[μ₃₀₁::Fractal] athena_kernel_v031.py

from __future__ import annotations

import os

import json

import math

import time

import copy

import hashlib

from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict, field

from datetime import datetime

from pathlib import Path

from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional, Tuple

# ============================================================

# CANONICAL ORDERS

# ============================================================

VECTOR_ORDER = ["L", "S", "T", "C", "A", "N", "U", "R", "M", "P", "H", "Z"]

QUALITY_ORDER = [

    "truth", "coherence", "novelty", "utility",

    "compression", "safety", "vitality", "recoverability"

]

SHADOW_ORDER = [

    "hallucination", "fragility", "drift", "ambiguity",

    "coupling", "vanity", "noise", "loop_risk"

]

# ============================================================

# BASIC UTILS

# ============================================================

def clamp01(x: float) -> float:

    return max(0.0, min(1.0, float(x)))

def squash(x: float) -> float:

    return 1.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-x))

def mean(xs: List[float], default: float = 0.0) -> float:

    return sum(xs) / len(xs) if xs else default

def variance(xs: List[float], default: float = 0.0) -> float:

    if not xs:

        return default

    m = mean(xs)

    return sum((x - m) ** 2 for x in xs) / len(xs)

def now_iso() -> str:

    return datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z"

def ensure_dir(path: str | Path) -> None:

    Path(path).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def load_json(path: str | Path, default: Any) -> Any:

    p = Path(path)

    if not p.exists():

        return copy.deepcopy(default)

    try:

        with p.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:

            return json.load(f)

    except Exception:

        return copy.deepcopy(default)

def save_json(path: str | Path, obj: Any) -> None:

    p = Path(path)

    ensure_dir(p.parent)

    tmp = p.with_suffix(p.suffix + ".tmp")

    with tmp.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:

        json.dump(obj, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

    tmp.replace(p)

def append_jsonl(path: str | Path, row: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:

    p = Path(path)

    ensure_dir(p.parent)

    with p.open("a", encoding="utf-8") as f:

        f.write(json.dumps(row, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")

def read_jsonl(path: str | Path, limit: int = 200) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:

    p = Path(path)

    if not p.exists():

        return []

    rows = []

    with p.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:

        for line in f:

            line = line.strip()

            if not line:

                continue

            try:

                rows.append(json.loads(line))

            except Exception:

                continue

    return rows[-limit:]

def sha256_bytes(b: bytes) -> str:

    return "sha256:" + hashlib.sha256(b).hexdigest()

def file_hash(path: str | Path) -> str:

    with open(path, "rb") as f:

        return sha256_bytes(f.read())

def shadow_total(shadow_vector: Dict[str, float]) -> float:

    return sum(float(shadow_vector.get(k, 0.0)) for k in SHADOW_ORDER) / max(1, len(SHADOW_ORDER))

def add_delta(x: Dict[str, float], delta_x: Dict[str, float], lam: float = 1.0) -> Dict[str, float]:

    out = dict(x)

    for k, v in delta_x.items():

        out[k] = clamp01(float(out.get(k, 0.0)) + lam * float(v))

    return out

def l2_distance_dict(a: Dict[str, float], b: Dict[str, float], order: List[str]) -> float:

    return math.sqrt(sum((float(a.get(k, 0.0)) - float(b.get(k, 0.0))) ** 2 for k in order))

def vector_dict_to_list(d: Dict[str, float], order: List[str]) -> List[float]:

    return [float(d.get(k, 0.0)) for k in order]

# ============================================================

# QUALITY / SHADOW

# ============================================================

QUALITY_WEIGHTS = {

    "truth": 1.00,

    "coherence": 0.95,

    "novelty": 0.72,

    "utility": 0.90,

    "compression": 0.78,

    "safety": 1.05,

    "vitality": 0.80,

    "recoverability": 1.00,

}

SHADOW_WEIGHTS = {

    "hallucination": 1.10,

    "fragility": 1.00,

    "drift": 0.90,

    "ambiguity": 0.95,

    "coupling": 0.82,

    "vanity": 0.76,

    "noise": 0.74,

    "loop_risk": 1.02,

}

def derive_quality_vector(vector: Dict[str, float]) -> Dict[str, float]:

    novelty_raw = 0.30 * (1.0 - vector["T"]) + 0.35 * vector["A"] + 0.35 * vector["P"]

    return {

        "truth": clamp01(0.35 * vector["L"] + 0.20 * vector["U"] + 0.20 * vector["N"] + 0.25 * vector["C"]),

        "coherence": clamp01(0.45 * vector["S"] + 0.20 * vector["C"] + 0.15 * vector["A"] + 0.20 * vector["Z"]),

        "novelty": clamp01(novelty_raw),

        "utility": clamp01(0.35 * vector["L"] + 0.25 * vector["C"] + 0.20 * vector["H"] + 0.20 * vector["M"]),

        "compression": clamp01(0.65 * vector["P"] + 0.35 * vector["Z"]),

        "safety": clamp01(0.20 * vector["N"] + 0.25 * vector["U"] + 0.25 * vector["H"] + 0.30 * vector["R"]),

        "vitality": clamp01(0.30 * vector["T"] + 0.20 * vector["A"] + 0.20 * vector["M"] + 0.30 * vector["Z"]),

        "recoverability": clamp01(0.65 * vector["H"] + 0.35 * vector["Z"]),

    }

def derive_shadow_vector(vector: Dict[str, float]) -> Dict[str, float]:

    return {

        "hallucination": clamp01(1.0 - 0.6 * vector["L"] - 0.4 * vector["U"]),

        "fragility": clamp01(1.0 - 0.7 * vector["H"] - 0.3 * vector["R"]),

        "drift": clamp01(1.0 - vector["T"]),

        "ambiguity": clamp01(1.0 - 0.5 * vector["L"] - 0.5 * vector["A"]),

        "coupling": clamp01(1.0 - 0.6 * vector["C"] - 0.4 * vector["S"]),

        "vanity": clamp01(1.0 - 0.5 * vector["N"] - 0.5 * vector["U"]),

        "noise": clamp01(1.0 - 0.5 * vector["P"] - 0.5 * vector["Z"]),

        "loop_risk": clamp01(1.0 - vector["R"]),

    }

def phi_quality(q: Dict[str, float]) -> float:

    return sum(float(q[k]) * QUALITY_WEIGHTS[k] for k in QUALITY_ORDER)

def phi_shadow(s: Dict[str, float]) -> float:

    return sum(float(s[k]) * SHADOW_WEIGHTS[k] for k in SHADOW_ORDER)

def phi_net(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:

    return phi_quality(state["quality_vector"]) - phi_shadow(state["shadow_vector"])

# ============================================================

# METRIC + CURVATURE

# ============================================================

def zeros(n: int) -> List[List[float]]:

    return [[0.0 for _ in range(n)] for _ in range(n)]

def symmetrize(M: List[List[float]]) -> List[List[float]]:

    n = len(M)

    out = zeros(n)

    for i in range(n):

        for j in range(n):

            out[i][j] = 0.5 * (M[i][j] + M[j][i])

    return out

def clamp_min_diag(M: List[List[float]], floor: float = 1e-3) -> List[List[float]]:

    out = [row[:] for row in M]

    for i in range(len(M)):

        if out[i][i] < floor:

            out[i][i] = floor

    return out

def build_metric_matrix(metric_state: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[List[float]]:

    idx = {k: i for i, k in enumerate(VECTOR_ORDER)}

    G = zeros(len(VECTOR_ORDER))

    for dim, val in metric_state.get("diagonal", {}).items():

        G[idx[dim]][idx[dim]] = float(val)

    for pair, val in metric_state.get("couplings", {}).items():

        left, right = pair.split(":")

        i, j = idx[left], idx[right]

        G[i][j] = float(val)

        G[j][i] = float(val)

    return clamp_min_diag(symmetrize(G))

def quad_form(v: List[float], G: List[List[float]]) -> float:

    total = 0.0

    n = len(v)

    for i in range(n):

        for j in range(n):

            total += v[i] * G[i][j] * v[j]

    return total

def movement_cost(delta_x: Dict[str, float], G: List[List[float]]) -> float:

    v = vector_dict_to_list(delta_x, VECTOR_ORDER)

    return math.sqrt(max(0.0, quad_form(v, G)))

def move_curvature_penalty(delta_x: Dict[str, float], K: Dict[str, Dict[str, float]]) -> float:

    dims = [k for k, v in delta_x.items() if abs(v) > 1e-12]

    total = 0.0

    for i in dims:

        for j in dims:

            if i == j:

                continue

            total += abs(float(delta_x[i]) * float(delta_x[j])) * float(K.get(i, {}).get(j, 0.0))

    return total

# ============================================================

# DEFAULT CONFIG

# ============================================================

DEFAULT_BASE_METRIC_STATE = {

    "diagonal": {

        "L": 1.00, "S": 1.10, "T": 1.05, "C": 1.15,

        "A": 0.95, "N": 1.00, "U": 0.95, "R": 1.20,

        "M": 1.00, "P": 1.05, "H": 1.10, "Z": 1.15,

    },

    "couplings": {

        "L:S": 0.18,

        "S:C": 0.21,

        "C:H": 0.24,

        "N:U": 0.19,

        "R:M": 0.22,

        "P:Z": 0.26,

        "H:Z": 0.17,

        "T:R": 0.16,

        "A:M": 0.12,

    },

}

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE = {

    d: {e: 0.0 for e in VECTOR_ORDER}

    for d in VECTOR_ORDER

}

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["R"]["M"] = DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["M"]["R"] = 0.40

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["C"]["H"] = DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["H"]["C"] = 0.31

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["P"]["Z"] = DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["Z"]["P"] = 0.28

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["T"]["R"] = DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["R"]["T"] = 0.25

DEFAULT_THRESHOLDS = {

    "corridor": {

        "min_truth": 0.62,

        "min_safety": 0.66,

        "min_recoverability": 0.64,

        "max_shadow_total": 0.35,

    }

}

DEFAULT_TUNNEL_THRESHOLDS = {

    "min_zero_point_clarity": 0.68,

    "min_compression_quality": 0.66,

    "min_repair_accessibility": 0.62,

    "curvature_trigger": 0.12,

    "max_invariant_loss": 0.08,

}

DEFAULT_MOVE_DELTA_MEMORY = {}

DEFAULT_MOVE_EFFICACY_MEMORY = {}

DEFAULT_METRIC_LEARNING_STATE = {k: {"observed_instability": 1.0, "count": 0} for k in VECTOR_ORDER}

DEFAULT_COUPLING_LEARNING_STATE = {}

DEFAULT_TUNNEL_LEARNING_STATE = {"global": {"count": 0, "mean_tunnel_advantage": 0.0}}

# ============================================================

# FILE PERSISTENCE + PATHS

# ============================================================

@dataclass

class RuntimePaths:

    root: Path

    artifacts_root: Path

    kernel_root: Path

    learned_root: Path

    witness_root: Path

    snapshots_root: Path

    config_root: Path

    move_delta_memory: Path

    move_efficacy_memory: Path

    metric_learning_state: Path

    coupling_learning_state: Path

    tunnel_learning_state: Path

    witness_jsonl: Path

    metric_prior: Path

    thresholds: Path

    tunnel_thresholds: Path

def build_runtime_paths(root: str = "athena_runtime") -> RuntimePaths:

    root_p = Path(root)

    return RuntimePaths(

        root=root_p,

        artifacts_root=root_p / "artifacts",

        kernel_root=root_p / "kernel",

        learned_root=root_p / "kernel" / "learned",

        witness_root=root_p / "kernel" / "witness",

        snapshots_root=root_p / "kernel" / "snapshots",

        config_root=root_p / "kernel" / "config",

        move_delta_memory=root_p / "kernel" / "learned" / "move_delta_memory.json",

        move_efficacy_memory=root_p / "kernel" / "learned" / "move_efficacy_memory.json",

        metric_learning_state=root_p / "kernel" / "learned" / "metric_learning_state.json",

        coupling_learning_state=root_p / "kernel" / "learned" / "coupling_learning_state.json",

        tunnel_learning_state=root_p / "kernel" / "learned" / "tunnel_learning_state.json",

        witness_jsonl=root_p / "kernel" / "witness" / "witness.jsonl",

        metric_prior=root_p / "kernel" / "config" / "metric_prior.json",

        thresholds=root_p / "kernel" / "config" / "thresholds.json",

        tunnel_thresholds=root_p / "kernel" / "config" / "tunnel_thresholds.json",

    )

def bootstrap_runtime(paths: RuntimePaths) -> None:

    ensure_dir(paths.artifacts_root / "code")

    ensure_dir(paths.artifacts_root / "manuscripts")

    ensure_dir(paths.artifacts_root / "witness")

    ensure_dir(paths.artifacts_root / "state")

    ensure_dir(paths.learned_root)

    ensure_dir(paths.witness_root)

    ensure_dir(paths.snapshots_root)

    ensure_dir(paths.config_root)

    if not paths.metric_prior.exists():

        save_json(paths.metric_prior, DEFAULT_BASE_METRIC_STATE)

    if not paths.thresholds.exists():

        save_json(paths.thresholds, DEFAULT_THRESHOLDS)

    if not paths.tunnel_thresholds.exists():

        save_json(paths.tunnel_thresholds, DEFAULT_TUNNEL_THRESHOLDS)

    if not paths.move_delta_memory.exists():

        save_json(paths.move_delta_memory, DEFAULT_MOVE_DELTA_MEMORY)

    if not paths.move_efficacy_memory.exists():

        save_json(paths.move_efficacy_memory, DEFAULT_MOVE_EFFICACY_MEMORY)

    if not paths.metric_learning_state.exists():

        save_json(paths.metric_learning_state, DEFAULT_METRIC_LEARNING_STATE)

    if not paths.coupling_learning_state.exists():

        save_json(paths.coupling_learning_state, DEFAULT_COUPLING_LEARNING_STATE)

    if not paths.tunnel_learning_state.exists():

        save_json(paths.tunnel_learning_state, DEFAULT_TUNNEL_LEARNING_STATE)

def seed_demo_files(paths: RuntimePaths) -> None:

    code_file = paths.artifacts_root / "code" / "gateway_demo.py"

    md_file = paths.artifacts_root / "manuscripts" / "chapter_demo.md"

    if not code_file.exists():

        code_file.write_text(

            "def watch_folder(path):\n"

            "    files = []\n"

            "    for name in os.listdir(path):\n"

            "        files.append(name)\n"

            "    return files\n",

            encoding="utf-8"

        )

    if not md_file.exists():

        md_file.write_text(

            "# Demo Chapter\n\n"

            "This section discusses the bridge process.\n\n"

            "The corridor matters.\n",

            encoding="utf-8"

        )

# ============================================================

# ARTIFACT DISCOVERY

# ============================================================

def discover_artifacts(root: str | Path) -> List[Path]:

    allowed_ext = {".py", ".md", ".txt", ".json", ".jsonl", ".yaml", ".yml"}

    out: List[Path] = []

    for dirpath, _dirnames, filenames in os.walk(root):

        for fn in filenames:

            p = Path(dirpath) / fn

            if p.suffix.lower() in allowed_ext:

                out.append(p)

    out.sort()

    return out

# ============================================================

# ADAPTERS

# ============================================================

class ArtifactAdapter:

    name = "base"

    @classmethod

    def can_handle(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        return False

    @classmethod

    def load(cls, path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        raise NotImplementedError

    @classmethod

    def extract_vector(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any], history: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        raise NotImplementedError

    @classmethod

    def generate_candidate_moves(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any]) -> List["CandidateMove"]:

        return []

    @classmethod

    def apply_move(cls, path: Path, move: "CandidateMove") -> Dict[str, Any]:

        raise NotImplementedError

    @classmethod

    def basic_parse_ok(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        try:

            cls.load(path)

            return True

        except Exception:

            return False

    @classmethod

    def snapshot(cls, path: Path, snapshot_root: Path) -> str:

        ts = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H-%M-%SZ")

        ensure_dir(snapshot_root / ts)

        safe_name = str(path).replace("/", "__").replace("\\", "__")

        snap = snapshot_root / ts / f"{safe_name}.bak"

        with open(path, "rb") as src, open(snap, "wb") as dst:

            dst.write(src.read())

        return str(snap)

    @classmethod

    def restore_snapshot(cls, snapshot_ref: str, path: Path) -> None:

        with open(snapshot_ref, "rb") as src, open(path, "wb") as dst:

            dst.write(src.read())

class CodeAdapter(ArtifactAdapter):

    name = "code"

    @classmethod

    def can_handle(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        return path.suffix.lower() in {".py", ".js", ".ts"}

    @classmethod

    def load(cls, path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

        lines = text.splitlines()

        return {

            "text": text,

            "lines": lines,

            "line_count": len(lines),

            "function_lines": [ln for ln in lines if ln.strip().startswith("def ") or ln.strip().startswith("function ")],

            "class_lines": [ln for ln in lines if ln.strip().startswith("class ")],

            "comment_lines": [ln for ln in lines if ln.strip().startswith("#") or ln.strip().startswith("//")],

            "imports": [ln for ln in lines if ln.strip().startswith("import ") or ln.strip().startswith("from ")],

            "has_module_docstring": text.strip().startswith('"""') or text.strip().startswith("'''"),

        }

    @classmethod

    def extract_vector(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any], history: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        line_count = max(1, content["line_count"])

        comment_ratio = len(content["comment_lines"]) / line_count

        import_count = len(content["imports"])

        fn_count = len(content["function_lines"])

        class_count = len(content["class_lines"])

        text = content["text"]

        explicit_fields_present = 1 if content["has_module_docstring"] else 0

        explicit_fields_expected = 1

        ambiguous_labels = text.count("TODO") + text.count("???")

        undefined_refs = text.count("pass")

        duplication = max(0, fn_count - len(set(content["function_lines"])))

        orphan_nodes = 1 if fn_count == 0 and class_count == 0 else 0

        invalid_nesting = 1 if line_count > 220 and fn_count <= 1 else 0

        recent_gain = 0.2 if history else 0.0

        recent_regression = 0.0

        change_entropy = 0.1 if line_count > 160 else 0.02

        hidden_deps = max(0, import_count - 5)

        unexplained_effects = 1 if "os.system(" in text or "subprocess" in text else 0

        broken_links = 1 if "NameError" in text else 0

        role_scores = {

            "bridge": 0.75 if "watch" in text or "copy" in text else 0.35,

            "witness": 0.70 if "hash" in text or "log" in text else 0.30,

            "guard": 0.65 if "validate" in text or "allow" in text else 0.25,

        }

        role_confusion_penalty = 0.05 if len([v for v in role_scores.values() if v > 0.6]) > 2 else 0.0

        identified_failure_modes = int("except" in text) + int("if" in text and "return" in text)

        expected_failure_modes = 3

        shadow_blindness_penalty = 0.12 if "except" not in text else 0.03

        claimed_confidence = 0.75 if content["has_module_docstring"] else 0.50

        support_confidence = 0.60 + min(0.25, comment_ratio)

        degradation_under_iteration = 0.10 if line_count > 180 else 0.03

        loop_blowup = 0.12 if "while True" in text and "seen" not in text else 0.03

        agent_scores = [0.65, 0.70, 0.58, 0.72]

        compression_fidelity = 0.75 if fn_count <= 5 else 0.58

        compression_compactness = 0.68 if line_count < 140 else 0.42

        compression_lossy_risk = 0.18 if line_count > 200 else 0.07

        repair_cost = 0.18 if line_count < 120 else 0.36

        rollback_difficulty = 0.10

        irreversibility = 0.05

        seed_clarity = 0.78 if fn_count <= 5 else 0.56

        invariant_preservation = 0.73 if "validate" in text or "log" in text else 0.51

        collapse_distortion = 0.12 if line_count > 220 else 0.05

        vector = {

            "L": clamp01((explicit_fields_present / explicit_fields_expected) - 0.08 * ambiguous_labels - 0.10 * undefined_refs),

            "S": clamp01(1.0 - 0.10 * duplication - 0.18 * orphan_nodes - 0.18 * invalid_nesting),

            "T": clamp01(squash(3.0 * (recent_gain - recent_regression - change_entropy))),

            "C": clamp01(1.0 - 0.10 * hidden_deps - 0.14 * unexplained_effects - 0.14 * broken_links),

            "A": clamp01(max(role_scores.values()) - role_confusion_penalty),

            "N": clamp01((identified_failure_modes / expected_failure_modes) - shadow_blindness_penalty),

            "U": clamp01(1.0 - abs(claimed_confidence - support_confidence)),

            "R": clamp01(1.0 - 0.6 * degradation_under_iteration - 0.8 * loop_blowup),

            "M": clamp01(mean(agent_scores) - 0.5 * variance(agent_scores)),

            "P": clamp01(0.45 * compression_fidelity + 0.35 * compression_compactness - 0.30 * compression_lossy_risk),

            "H": clamp01(1.0 - (0.45 * repair_cost + 0.35 * rollback_difficulty + 0.45 * irreversibility)),

            "Z": clamp01(0.45 * seed_clarity + 0.40 * invariant_preservation - 0.40 * collapse_distortion),

        }

        return {

            "artifact_id": str(path.relative_to(path.parents[1])),

            "artifact_type": cls.name,

            "path": str(path),

            "vector": vector,

            "quality_vector": derive_quality_vector(vector),

            "shadow_vector": derive_shadow_vector(vector),

            "invariants": {

                "role": "code",

                "reversible": True,

            },

        }

    @classmethod

    def generate_candidate_moves(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any]) -> List["CandidateMove"]:

        moves: List[CandidateMove] = []

        text = content["text"]

        if not content["has_module_docstring"]:

            moves.append(CandidateMove(

                move_id="code_add_module_docstring",

                title="Add bounded module docstring",

                move_type="code_clarify",

                delta_x={"L": 0.08, "S": 0.02, "P": 0.02, "H": 0.01},

                drift_risk=0.01,

                repetition_penalty=0.00,

                seed_gain=0.04,

                curvature_penalty_hint=0.02,

                target_template="default_template",

            ))

        if len(content["function_lines"]) > 0 and "# invariant:" not in text.lower():

            moves.append(CandidateMove(

                move_id="code_add_invariant_comment",

                title="Add one bounded invariant comment",

                move_type="code_repair",

                delta_x={"H": 0.06, "Z": 0.03, "L": 0.03, "N": 0.01},

                drift_risk=0.02,

                repetition_penalty=0.01,

                seed_gain=0.06,

                curvature_penalty_hint=0.03,

                target_template="repair_template",

            ))

        return moves

    @classmethod

    def apply_move(cls, path: Path, move: "CandidateMove") -> Dict[str, Any]:

        text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

        if move.move_id == "code_add_module_docstring":

            if not text.strip().startswith('"""') and not text.strip().startswith("'''"):

                doc = '"""\nAthena kernel managed file: bounded module docstring.\n"""\n\n'

                text = doc + text

        elif move.move_id == "code_add_invariant_comment":

            if "# invariant:" not in text.lower():

                lines = text.splitlines()

                inserted = False

                out = []

                for ln in lines:

                    out.append(ln)

                    if (ln.strip().startswith("def ") or ln.strip().startswith("function ")) and not inserted:

                        indent = "    " if ln.strip().startswith("def ") else "  "

                        out.append(f"{indent}# invariant: preserve bounded reversible behavior")

                        inserted = True

                text = "\n".join(out) + ("\n" if not text.endswith("\n") else "")

        path.write_text(text, encoding="utf-8")

        return {"status": "ok", "move_id": move.move_id}

class MarkdownAdapter(ArtifactAdapter):

    name = "manuscript"

    @classmethod

    def can_handle(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        return path.suffix.lower() in {".md", ".txt"}

    @classmethod

    def load(cls, path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

        lines = text.splitlines()

        headings = [ln for ln in lines if ln.strip().startswith("#")]

        return {

            "text": text,

            "lines": lines,

            "line_count": len(lines),

            "headings": headings,

            "paragraphs": [p for p in text.split("\n\n") if p.strip()],

        }

    @classmethod

    def extract_vector(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any], history: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        text = content["text"]

        heading_count = len(content["headings"])

        para_count = len(content["paragraphs"])

        line_count = max(1, content["line_count"])

        explicit_fields_present = 1 if heading_count > 0 else 0

        explicit_fields_expected = 1

        ambiguous_labels = text.lower().count("something") + text.lower().count("stuff")

        undefined_refs = text.lower().count("it") if len(text) < 100 else max(0, text.lower().count("it") - 3)

        duplication = max(0, para_count - len(set(p.strip() for p in content["paragraphs"])))

        orphan_nodes = 1 if heading_count == 0 else 0

        invalid_nesting = 1 if any(h.count("#") > 4 for h in content["headings"]) else 0

        recent_gain = 0.15 if history else 0.0

        recent_regression = 0.0

        change_entropy = 0.07 if line_count > 180 else 0.03

        hidden_deps = 0

        unexplained_effects = 1 if "corridor" in text.lower() and "definition" not in text.lower() else 0

        broken_links = 0

        role_scores = {

            "scaffold": 0.70 if heading_count > 0 else 0.35,

            "seed": 0.62 if "summary" in text.lower() or "seed" in text.lower() else 0.30,

            "witness": 0.58 if "observe" in text.lower() or "witness" in text.lower() else 0.25,

        }

        role_confusion_penalty = 0.03 if len([v for v in role_scores.values() if v > 0.6]) > 2 else 0.0

        identified_failure_modes = int("warning" in text.lower()) + int("avoid" in text.lower())

        expected_failure_modes = 2

        shadow_blindness_penalty = 0.10 if identified_failure_modes == 0 else 0.02

        claimed_confidence = 0.72 if heading_count > 0 else 0.52

        support_confidence = 0.60 + min(0.2, heading_count * 0.03)

        degradation_under_iteration = 0.05 if para_count < 12 else 0.14

        loop_blowup = 0.08 if text.lower().count("next") > 8 else 0.02

        agent_scores = [0.68, 0.74, 0.61, 0.66]

        compression_fidelity = 0.78 if para_count <= 8 else 0.55

        compression_compactness = 0.71 if line_count < 140 else 0.46

        compression_lossy_risk = 0.09 if heading_count > 0 else 0.18

        repair_cost = 0.12 if line_count < 160 else 0.28

        rollback_difficulty = 0.08

        irreversibility = 0.03

        seed_clarity = 0.74 if heading_count > 0 else 0.48

        invariant_preservation = 0.67 if "definition" in text.lower() or "purpose" in text.lower() else 0.50

        collapse_distortion = 0.11 if para_count > 12 else 0.05

        vector = {

            "L": clamp01((explicit_fields_present / explicit_fields_expected) - 0.05 * ambiguous_labels - 0.05 * undefined_refs),

            "S": clamp01(1.0 - 0.10 * duplication - 0.18 * orphan_nodes - 0.10 * invalid_nesting),

            "T": clamp01(squash(3.0 * (recent_gain - recent_regression - change_entropy))),

            "C": clamp01(1.0 - 0.10 * hidden_deps - 0.12 * unexplained_effects - 0.12 * broken_links),

            "A": clamp01(max(role_scores.values()) - role_confusion_penalty),

            "N": clamp01((identified_failure_modes / expected_failure_modes) - shadow_blindness_penalty),

            "U": clamp01(1.0 - abs(claimed_confidence - support_confidence)),

            "R": clamp01(1.0 - 0.6 * degradation_under_iteration - 0.8 * loop_blowup),

            "M": clamp01(mean(agent_scores) - 0.5 * variance(agent_scores)),

            "P": clamp01(0.45 * compression_fidelity + 0.35 * compression_compactness - 0.30 * compression_lossy_risk),

            "H": clamp01(1.0 - (0.45 * repair_cost + 0.35 * rollback_difficulty + 0.45 * irreversibility)),

            "Z": clamp01(0.45 * seed_clarity + 0.40 * invariant_preservation - 0.40 * collapse_distortion),

        }

        return {

            "artifact_id": str(path.relative_to(path.parents[1])),

            "artifact_type": cls.name,

            "path": str(path),

            "vector": vector,

            "quality_vector": derive_quality_vector(vector),

            "shadow_vector": derive_shadow_vector(vector),

            "invariants": {

                "role": "manuscript",

                "reversible": True,

            },

        }

    @classmethod

    def generate_candidate_moves(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any]) -> List["CandidateMove"]:

        moves: List[CandidateMove] = []

        text = content["text"]

        if "Definition:" not in text and "corridor" in text.lower():

            moves.append(CandidateMove(

                move_id="md_add_definition",

                title="Add one bounded definition line",

                move_type="manuscript_clarify",

                delta_x={"L": 0.08, "U": 0.05, "A": 0.02, "N": 0.01},

                drift_risk=0.01,

                repetition_penalty=0.00,

                seed_gain=0.04,

                curvature_penalty_hint=0.02,

                target_template="default_template",

            ))

        if "## Seed Summary" not in text:

            moves.append(CandidateMove(

                move_id="md_add_seed_summary",

                title="Add one bounded seed summary section",

                move_type="manuscript_compress",

                delta_x={"P": 0.06, "Z": 0.04, "L": 0.03},

                drift_risk=0.015,

                repetition_penalty=0.01,

                seed_gain=0.07,

                curvature_penalty_hint=0.03,

                target_template="compression_template",

            ))

        return moves

    @classmethod

    def apply_move(cls, path: Path, move: "CandidateMove") -> Dict[str, Any]:

        text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

        if move.move_id == "md_add_definition":

            if "Definition:" not in text:

                insertion = "\nDefinition: Corridor = the bounded safe operating region for changes.\n"

                parts = text.splitlines()

                if parts and parts[0].startswith("#"):

                    parts.insert(1, insertion.strip("\n"))

                    text = "\n".join(parts) + "\n"

                else:

                    text += insertion

        elif move.move_id == "md_add_seed_summary":

            if "## Seed Summary" not in text:

                addition = "\n## Seed Summary\n\n- Core theme preserved in bounded form.\n"

                text = text.rstrip() + addition + "\n"

        path.write_text(text, encoding="utf-8")

        return {"status": "ok", "move_id": move.move_id}

class WitnessAdapter(ArtifactAdapter):

    name = "witness"

    @classmethod

    def can_handle(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        return path.suffix.lower() == ".jsonl"

    @classmethod

    def load(cls, path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        rows = read_jsonl(path, limit=200)

        return {"rows": rows, "count": len(rows)}

    @classmethod

    def extract_vector(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any], history: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        rows = content["rows"]

        count = len(rows)

        required = ["move_id", "strategy", "x_before", "x_after", "efficacy"]

        present_counts = 0

        if rows:

            present_counts = sum(1 for k in required if k in rows[-1])

        explicit = present_counts / max(1, len(required))

        schema_consistency = 1.0 if all(isinstance(r, dict) for r in rows[-10:]) else 0.5

        efficacy_mean = mean([float(r.get("efficacy", 0.0)) for r in rows[-20:]], default=0.0)

        corridor_rate = mean([1.0 if r.get("corridor_ok", True) else 0.0 for r in rows[-20:]], default=1.0)

        vector = {

            "L": clamp01(explicit),

            "S": clamp01(schema_consistency),

            "T": clamp01(0.5 + 0.2 * efficacy_mean),

            "C": clamp01(0.6 + 0.2 * corridor_rate),

            "A": 0.65,

            "N": 0.70 if count > 0 else 0.40,

            "U": 0.75,

            "R": clamp01(0.55 + 0.2 * corridor_rate),

            "M": 0.60,

            "P": clamp01(0.50 + min(0.25, count * 0.01)),

            "H": clamp01(0.55 + 0.2 * corridor_rate),

            "Z": clamp01(0.50 + min(0.20, count * 0.008)),

        }

        return {

            "artifact_id": str(path.relative_to(path.parents[1])),

            "artifact_type": cls.name,

            "path": str(path),

            "vector": vector,

            "quality_vector": derive_quality_vector(vector),

            "shadow_vector": derive_shadow_vector(vector),

            "invariants": {"role": "witness", "reversible": True},

        }

class StateAdapter(ArtifactAdapter):

    name = "state"

    @classmethod

    def can_handle(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        return path.suffix.lower() in {".json", ".yaml", ".yml"} and "learned" not in str(path)

    @classmethod

    def load(cls, path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        if path.suffix.lower() == ".json":

            return load_json(path, {})

        return {"raw_text": path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")}

    @classmethod

    def extract_vector(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any], history: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        keys = list(content.keys()) if isinstance(content, dict) else []

        vector = {

            "L": clamp01(0.55 + 0.02 * len(keys)),

            "S": 0.72 if isinstance(content, dict) else 0.45,

            "T": 0.58,

            "C": 0.62,

            "A": 0.60,

            "N": 0.55,

            "U": 0.66,

            "R": 0.61,

            "M": 0.58,

            "P": 0.65,

            "H": 0.70,

            "Z": 0.64,

        }

        return {

            "artifact_id": str(path.relative_to(path.parents[1])),

            "artifact_type": cls.name,

            "path": str(path),

            "vector": vector,

            "quality_vector": derive_quality_vector(vector),

            "shadow_vector": derive_shadow_vector(vector),

            "invariants": {"role": "state", "reversible": True},

        }

ADAPTERS = [WitnessAdapter, StateAdapter, CodeAdapter, MarkdownAdapter]

def choose_adapter(path: Path) -> Optional[type[ArtifactAdapter]]:

    for adapter in ADAPTERS:

        if adapter.can_handle(path):

            return adapter

    return None

# ============================================================

# CANDIDATE / LEARNING MEMORY

# ============================================================

@dataclass

class CandidateMove:

    move_id: str

    title: str

    move_type: str

    delta_x: Dict[str, float]

    drift_risk: float

    repetition_penalty: float

    seed_gain: float

    curvature_penalty_hint: float = 0.0

    target_template: str = "default_template"

    reversible: bool = True

    corridor_safe_hint: bool = True

@dataclass

class KernelDecision:

    move_id: str

    title: str

    strategy: str

    direct_score: float

    tunnel_score: float

    final_score: float

    projected_lambda: float

    notes: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)

def blended_delta_x(candidate_delta_x, move_memory_entry, kappa0=5.0):

    if not move_memory_entry:

        return dict(candidate_delta_x)

    count = float(move_memory_entry.get("count", 0))

    mean_dx = move_memory_entry.get("mean_delta_x", {})

    var_dx = move_memory_entry.get("variance_delta_x", {})

    avg_var = sum(float(var_dx.get(k, 0.0)) for k in VECTOR_ORDER) / len(VECTOR_ORDER)

    conf = (count / (count + kappa0)) * (1.0 / (1.0 + avg_var))

    out = {}

    for k in VECTOR_ORDER:

        templ = float(candidate_delta_x.get(k, 0.0))

        learned = float(mean_dx.get(k, templ))

        out[k] = (1 - conf) * templ + conf * learned

    return out

def efficacy_prior_bonus(move_id: str, move_efficacy_memory: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[float, float]:

    entry = move_efficacy_memory.get(move_id)

    if not entry:

        return 0.0, 0.0

    return float(entry.get("mean_efficacy", 0.0)), float(entry.get("variance_efficacy", 0.0))

def tunnel_advantage_prior(move_id: str, tunnel_learning_state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:

    entry = tunnel_learning_state.get(move_id)

    if not entry:

        return float(tunnel_learning_state.get("global", {}).get("mean_tunnel_advantage", 0.0))

    return float(entry.get("mean_tunnel_advantage", 0.0))

def build_learned_metric_state(

    base_metric_state: Dict[str, Any],

    metric_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

    coupling_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

    eta_diag: float = 0.35,

    eta_coup: float = 0.45

) -> Dict[str, Any]:

    out = {

        "diagonal": dict(base_metric_state.get("diagonal", {})),

        "couplings": dict(base_metric_state.get("couplings", {})),

    }

    for dim in VECTOR_ORDER:

        base = float(out["diagonal"].get(dim, 1.0))

        learned = float(metric_learning_state.get(dim, {}).get("observed_instability", base))

        out["diagonal"][dim] = max(1e-3, (1 - eta_diag) * base + eta_diag * learned)

    for pair, entry in coupling_learning_state.items():

        base = float(out["couplings"].get(pair, 0.0))

        learned = float(entry.get("observed_coupling", base))

        out["couplings"][pair] = (1 - eta_coup) * base + eta_coup * learned

    return out

def build_learned_curvature_state(base_curvature_state, tunnel_learning_state):

    return copy.deepcopy(base_curvature_state)

# ============================================================

# CORRIDOR + TUNNEL

# ============================================================

def inside_corridor(candidate_state: Dict[str, Any], thresholds: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:

    q = candidate_state["quality_vector"]

    s = candidate_state["shadow_vector"]

    c = thresholds["corridor"]

    return (

        float(q["truth"]) >= float(c["min_truth"]) and

        float(q["safety"]) >= float(c["min_safety"]) and

        float(q["recoverability"]) >= float(c["min_recoverability"]) and

        shadow_total(s) <= float(c["max_shadow_total"])

    )

def shrink_back_projection(

    x: Dict[str, float],

    delta_x: Dict[str, float],

    evaluator,

    thresholds: Dict[str, Any],

    steps: int,

    artifact_id: str

) -> Optional[Tuple[float, Dict[str, Any]]]:

    for n in range(steps, -1, -1):

        lam = n / max(steps, 1)

        candidate_vec = add_delta(x, delta_x, lam)

        candidate_state = evaluator(candidate_vec, artifact_id=artifact_id)

        if inside_corridor(candidate_state, thresholds):

            return lam, candidate_state

    return None

def should_tunnel(candidate: CandidateMove, current_state: Dict[str, Any], tunnel_thresholds: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:

    vector = current_state["vector"]

    return (

        float(candidate.curvature_penalty_hint) >= float(tunnel_thresholds["curvature_trigger"]) and

        float(vector["Z"]) >= float(tunnel_thresholds["min_zero_point_clarity"]) and

        float(vector["P"]) >= float(tunnel_thresholds["min_compression_quality"]) and

        float(vector["H"]) >= float(tunnel_thresholds["min_repair_accessibility"])

    )

def collapse_to_seed(current_state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

    vec = current_state["vector"]

    return {

        "seed_id": f"{current_state.get('artifact_id', 'artifact')}_seed",

        "invariants": copy.deepcopy(current_state.get("invariants", {})),

        "compressed_vector": {

            "L": vec["L"], "S": vec["S"], "C": vec["C"],

            "P": vec["P"], "H": vec["H"], "Z": vec["Z"],

        },

    }

def expand_from_seed(seed: Dict[str, Any], target_template: str = "default_template") -> Dict[str, float]:

    base = {k: 0.5 for k in VECTOR_ORDER}

    for k, v in seed.get("compressed_vector", {}).items():

        base[k] = clamp01(v)

    if target_template == "repair_template":

        base["H"] = clamp01(base["H"] + 0.05)

        base["Z"] = clamp01(base["Z"] + 0.03)

        base["N"] = clamp01(base["N"] + 0.02)

    elif target_template == "compression_template":

        base["P"] = clamp01(base["P"] + 0.05)

        base["Z"] = clamp01(base["Z"] + 0.03)

    elif target_template == "event_bus_bridge_template":

        base["S"] = clamp01(base["S"] + 0.04)

        base["C"] = clamp01(base["C"] + 0.03)

        base["R"] = clamp01(base["R"] - 0.01)

        base["M"] = clamp01(base["M"] + 0.02)

    return base

def invariant_loss_penalty(seed: Dict[str, Any], expanded_vector: Dict[str, float]) -> float:

    comp = seed.get("compressed_vector", {})

    if not comp:

        return 0.0

    total = 0.0

    for k, v in comp.items():

        total += abs(float(v) - float(expanded_vector.get(k, 0.0)))

    return total / len(comp)

def tunnel_score(

    current_state: Dict[str, Any],

    candidate: CandidateMove,

    evaluator

) -> Tuple[float, Dict[str, Any]]:

    seed = collapse_to_seed(current_state)

    expanded_vec = expand_from_seed(seed, candidate.target_template)

    expanded_state = evaluator(expanded_vec, artifact_id=current_state["artifact_id"])

    current_q = sum(current_state["quality_vector"].values())

    new_q = sum(expanded_state["quality_vector"].values())

    current_s = sum(current_state["shadow_vector"].values())

    new_s = sum(expanded_state["shadow_vector"].values())

    q_gain = new_q - current_q

    s_relief = current_s - new_s

    collapse_cost = 0.03

    expand_cost = 0.05

    inv_pen = invariant_loss_penalty(seed, expanded_vec)

    return q_gain + s_relief - collapse_cost - expand_cost - inv_pen, expanded_state

# ============================================================

# LEARNING UPDATES

# ============================================================

def update_move_delta_memory(memory, move_id, delta_x_empirical, alpha=0.2):

    entry = memory.setdefault(move_id, {

        "count": 0,

        "mean_delta_x": {k: 0.0 for k in VECTOR_ORDER},

        "variance_delta_x": {k: 0.0 for k in VECTOR_ORDER},

    })

    entry["count"] += 1

    for k in VECTOR_ORDER:

        old_mean = float(entry["mean_delta_x"][k])

        x = float(delta_x_empirical.get(k, 0.0))

        new_mean = (1 - alpha) * old_mean + alpha * x

        old_var = float(entry["variance_delta_x"][k])

        new_var = (1 - alpha) * old_var + alpha * (x - new_mean) ** 2

        entry["mean_delta_x"][k] = new_mean

        entry["variance_delta_x"][k] = new_var

    return memory

def update_move_efficacy_memory(memory, move_id, strategy, efficacy, corridor_ok, alpha=0.2):

    entry = memory.setdefault(move_id, {

        "count": 0,

        "mean_efficacy": 0.0,

        "variance_efficacy": 0.0,

        "corridor_success_rate": 1.0,

        "strategy_breakdown": {}

    })

    entry["count"] += 1

    old_mean = float(entry["mean_efficacy"])

    new_mean = (1 - alpha) * old_mean + alpha * efficacy

    old_var = float(entry["variance_efficacy"])

    new_var = (1 - alpha) * old_var + alpha * (efficacy - new_mean) ** 2

    old_corr = float(entry["corridor_success_rate"])

    new_corr = (1 - alpha) * old_corr + alpha * (1.0 if corridor_ok else 0.0)

    entry["mean_efficacy"] = new_mean

    entry["variance_efficacy"] = new_var

    entry["corridor_success_rate"] = new_corr

    strat = entry["strategy_breakdown"].setdefault(strategy, {"count": 0, "mean_efficacy": 0.0})

    strat["count"] += 1

    strat["mean_efficacy"] = (1 - alpha) * float(strat["mean_efficacy"]) + alpha * efficacy

    return memory

def update_metric_learning_state(metric_learning, delta_x_empirical, shadow_delta, alpha=0.2):

    shadow_up = sum(max(float(v), 0.0) for v in shadow_delta.values())

    for k in VECTOR_ORDER:

        entry = metric_learning.setdefault(k, {"observed_instability": 1.0, "count": 0})

        entry["count"] += 1

        signal = abs(float(delta_x_empirical.get(k, 0.0))) * (1.0 + shadow_up)

        old = float(entry["observed_instability"])

        entry["observed_instability"] = (1 - alpha) * old + alpha * max(1e-3, signal)

    return metric_learning

def update_coupling_learning_state(coupling_learning, delta_x_empirical, shadow_delta, alpha=0.2):

    shadow_up = sum(max(float(v), 0.0) for v in shadow_delta.values())

    for i_idx, i in enumerate(VECTOR_ORDER):

        for j in VECTOR_ORDER[i_idx + 1:]:

            pair = f"{i}:{j}"

            entry = coupling_learning.setdefault(pair, {"observed_coupling": 0.0, "count": 0})

            entry["count"] += 1

            signal = abs(float(delta_x_empirical.get(i, 0.0)) * float(delta_x_empirical.get(j, 0.0))) * (1.0 + shadow_up)

            old = float(entry["observed_coupling"])

            entry["observed_coupling"] = (1 - alpha) * old + alpha * signal

    return coupling_learning

def update_tunnel_learning_state(tunnel_learning, move_id, strategy, direct_score, tunnel_score_val, efficacy, alpha=0.2):

    global_entry = tunnel_learning.setdefault("global", {"count": 0, "mean_tunnel_advantage": 0.0})

    move_entry = tunnel_learning.setdefault(move_id, {"count": 0, "mean_tunnel_advantage": 0.0, "tunnel_success_rate": 0.5})

    adv = float(tunnel_score_val) - float(direct_score)

    for entry in (global_entry, move_entry):

        entry["count"] += 1

        old = float(entry["mean_tunnel_advantage"])

        entry["mean_tunnel_advantage"] = (1 - alpha) * old + alpha * adv

    if strategy == "tunnel":

        old_sr = float(move_entry["tunnel_success_rate"])

        move_entry["tunnel_success_rate"] = (1 - alpha) * old_sr + alpha * (1.0 if efficacy > 0 else 0.0)

    return tunnel_learning

def apply_witness_learning(

    witness_row,

    move_delta_memory,

    move_efficacy_memory,

    metric_learning_state,

    coupling_learning_state,

    tunnel_learning_state,

    alpha=0.2

):

    move_id = witness_row["move_id"]

    strategy = witness_row["strategy"]

    efficacy = float(witness_row["efficacy"])

    corridor_ok = bool(witness_row.get("corridor_ok", True))

    delta_x_empirical = witness_row["delta_x_empirical"]

    shadow_delta = witness_row["shadow_delta"]

    direct_score = float(witness_row.get("direct_score", 0.0))

    tunnel_score_val = float(witness_row.get("tunnel_score", 0.0))

    update_move_delta_memory(move_delta_memory, move_id, delta_x_empirical, alpha=alpha)

    update_move_efficacy_memory(move_efficacy_memory, move_id, strategy, efficacy, corridor_ok, alpha=alpha)

    update_metric_learning_state(metric_learning_state, delta_x_empirical, shadow_delta, alpha=alpha)

    update_coupling_learning_state(coupling_learning_state, delta_x_empirical, shadow_delta, alpha=alpha)

    update_tunnel_learning_state(tunnel_learning_state, move_id, strategy, direct_score, tunnel_score_val, efficacy, alpha=alpha)

# ============================================================

# VALIDATION

# ============================================================

def validate_real_artifact(path: Path, adapter: type[ArtifactAdapter], state: Dict[str, Any], thresholds: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:

    return path.exists() and adapter.basic_parse_ok(path) and inside_corridor(state, thresholds)

# ============================================================

# NAVIGATOR

# ============================================================

class NavigatorV031:

    def __init__(

        self,

        base_metric_state: Dict[str, Any],

        base_curvature_state: Dict[str, Dict[str, float]],

        thresholds: Dict[str, Any],

        tunnel_thresholds: Dict[str, Any],

        move_delta_memory: Dict[str, Any],

        move_efficacy_memory: Dict[str, Any],

        metric_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

        coupling_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

        tunnel_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

    ) -> None:

        self.thresholds = thresholds

        self.tunnel_thresholds = tunnel_thresholds

        self.move_delta_memory = move_delta_memory

        self.move_efficacy_memory = move_efficacy_memory

        self.metric_learning_state = metric_learning_state

        self.coupling_learning_state = coupling_learning_state

        self.tunnel_learning_state = tunnel_learning_state

        self.metric_state = build_learned_metric_state(

            base_metric_state,

            metric_learning_state,

            coupling_learning_state

        )

        self.curvature_state = build_learned_curvature_state(

            base_curvature_state,

            tunnel_learning_state

        )

        self.G = build_metric_matrix(self.metric_state)

    def choose_best_move(self, current_state: Dict[str, Any], candidates: List[CandidateMove]) -> Optional[Tuple[KernelDecision, CandidateMove, Dict[str, float]]]:

        best = None

        best_score = float("-inf")

        artifact_id = current_state["artifact_id"]

        def local_eval(vec: Dict[str, float], artifact_id: str = artifact_id) -> Dict[str, Any]:

            return evaluate_vector(vec, artifact_id=artifact_id)

        for candidate in candidates:

            learned_entry = self.move_delta_memory.get(candidate.move_id)

            used_delta_x = blended_delta_x(candidate.delta_x, learned_entry)

            geom_cost = movement_cost(used_delta_x, self.G)

            curv_pen = move_curvature_penalty(used_delta_x, self.curvature_state) + candidate.curvature_penalty_hint

            projection = shrink_back_projection(

                current_state["vector"],

                used_delta_x,

                local_eval,

                self.thresholds,

                steps=12,

                artifact_id=artifact_id

            )

            if projection is None:

                direct_score = float("-inf")

                lam = 0.0

            else:

                lam, projected_state = projection

                projected_gain = phi_net(projected_state) - phi_net(current_state)

                eff_prior, eff_var = efficacy_prior_bonus(candidate.move_id, self.move_efficacy_memory)

                direct_score = (

                    projected_gain

                    - geom_cost

                    - curv_pen

                    - float(candidate.drift_risk)

                    - float(candidate.repetition_penalty)

                    + float(candidate.seed_gain)

                    + 0.15 * eff_prior

                    - 0.10 * eff_var

                )

                if lam < 1.0:

                    direct_score *= lam

            tunnel_score_val = float("-inf")

            if should_tunnel(candidate, current_state, self.tunnel_thresholds):

                tunnel_score_raw, _ = tunnel_score(current_state, candidate, local_eval)

                tunnel_score_val = tunnel_score_raw + 0.20 * tunnel_advantage_prior(candidate.move_id, self.tunnel_learning_state)

            if tunnel_score_val > direct_score:

                strategy = "tunnel"

                final_score = tunnel_score_val

            else:

                strategy = "direct"

                final_score = direct_score

            if final_score > best_score:

                best_score = final_score

                best = (

                    KernelDecision(

                        move_id=candidate.move_id,

                        title=candidate.title,

                        strategy=strategy,

                        direct_score=direct_score,

                        tunnel_score=tunnel_score_val,

                        final_score=final_score,

                        projected_lambda=lam if projection else 0.0,

                        notes={

                            "geom_cost": geom_cost,

                            "curvature_penalty": curv_pen,

                            "seed_gain": candidate.seed_gain,

                            "used_delta_x": used_delta_x,

                        },

                    ),

                    candidate,

                    used_delta_x,

                )

        return best

# ============================================================

# WITNESS CHAIN

# ============================================================

def last_witness_hash(path: Path) -> str:

    rows = read_jsonl(path, limit=1)

    if not rows:

        return "GENESIS"

    return rows[-1].get("hash", "GENESIS")

def witness_hash(row: Dict[str, Any], prev_hash: str) -> str:

    payload = json.dumps(row, sort_keys=True, ensure_ascii=False).encode("utf-8")

    return sha256_bytes(prev_hash.encode("utf-8") + payload)

# ============================================================

# REAL KERNEL CYCLE

# ============================================================

def extract_state_for_artifact(path: Path, adapter: type[ArtifactAdapter], witness_rows: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

    content = adapter.load(path)

    history = [r for r in witness_rows if r.get("artifact_path") == str(path)]

    state = adapter.extract_vector(path, content, history)

    state["artifact_path"] = str(path)

    state["artifact_hash"] = file_hash(path)

    return state

def execute_one_artifact_cycle(

    path: Path,

    adapter: type[ArtifactAdapter],

    paths: RuntimePaths,

) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:

    witness_rows = read_jsonl(paths.witness_jsonl, limit=300)

    move_delta_memory = load_json(paths.move_delta_memory, DEFAULT_MOVE_DELTA_MEMORY)

    move_efficacy_memory = load_json(paths.move_efficacy_memory, DEFAULT_MOVE_EFFICACY_MEMORY)

    metric_learning_state = load_json(paths.metric_learning_state, DEFAULT_METRIC_LEARNING_STATE)

    coupling_learning_state = load_json(paths.coupling_learning_state, DEFAULT_COUPLING_LEARNING_STATE)

    tunnel_learning_state = load_json(paths.tunnel_learning_state, DEFAULT_TUNNEL_LEARNING_STATE)

    base_metric_state = load_json(paths.metric_prior, DEFAULT_BASE_METRIC_STATE)

    thresholds = load_json(paths.thresholds, DEFAULT_THRESHOLDS)

    tunnel_thresholds = load_json(paths.tunnel_thresholds, DEFAULT_TUNNEL_THRESHOLDS)

    current_state = extract_state_for_artifact(path, adapter, witness_rows)

    content = adapter.load(path)

    candidates = adapter.generate_candidate_moves(path, content)

    if not candidates:

        return None

    navigator = NavigatorV031(

        base_metric_state=base_metric_state,

        base_curvature_state=DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE,

        thresholds=thresholds,

        tunnel_thresholds=tunnel_thresholds,

        move_delta_memory=move_delta_memory,

        move_efficacy_memory=move_efficacy_memory,

        metric_learning_state=metric_learning_state,

        coupling_learning_state=coupling_learning_state,

        tunnel_learning_state=tunnel_learning_state,

    )

    chosen = navigator.choose_best_move(current_state, candidates)

    if chosen is None:

        return None

    decision, chosen_candidate, used_delta_x = chosen

    artifact_hash_before = current_state["artifact_hash"]

    snapshot_ref = adapter.snapshot(path, paths.snapshots_root)

    status = "ok"

    rollback_reason = None

    try:

        if decision.strategy == "direct":

            adapter.apply_move(path, chosen_candidate)

        else:

            # tunnel strategy still resolves to a bounded concrete move in v0.3.1

            adapter.apply_move(path, chosen_candidate)

        after_state = extract_state_for_artifact(path, adapter, witness_rows)

        corridor_ok = validate_real_artifact(path, adapter, after_state, thresholds)

        if not corridor_ok:

            adapter.restore_snapshot(snapshot_ref, path)

            status = "rollback"

            rollback_reason = "corridor_or_parse_validation_failed"

            after_state = extract_state_for_artifact(path, adapter, witness_rows)

        else:

            status = "applied"

    except Exception as e:

        adapter.restore_snapshot(snapshot_ref, path)

        status = "rollback"

        rollback_reason = f"exception:{type(e).__name__}"

        after_state = extract_state_for_artifact(path, adapter, witness_rows)

    delta_x_empirical = {

        k: round(float(after_state["vector"][k]) - float(current_state["vector"][k]), 6)

        for k in VECTOR_ORDER

    }

    quality_delta = {

        k: round(float(after_state["quality_vector"][k]) - float(current_state["quality_vector"][k]), 6)

        for k in QUALITY_ORDER

    }

    shadow_delta = {

        k: round(float(after_state["shadow_vector"][k]) - float(current_state["shadow_vector"][k]), 6)

        for k in SHADOW_ORDER

    }

    q_gain = sum(quality_delta.values())

    s_penalty = sum(max(v, 0.0) for v in shadow_delta.values())

    s_relief = -sum(min(v, 0.0) for v in shadow_delta.values())

    denom = 0.001 + abs(decision.notes.get("geom_cost", 0.0)) + abs(decision.notes.get("curvature_penalty", 0.0))

    efficacy = (q_gain + s_relief - s_penalty) / denom

    prev_hash = last_witness_hash(paths.witness_jsonl)

    base_row = {

        "ts": now_iso(),

        "artifact_id": current_state["artifact_id"],

        "artifact_path": str(path),

        "artifact_type": adapter.name,

        "artifact_hash_before": artifact_hash_before,

        "artifact_hash_after": after_state["artifact_hash"],

        "move_id": decision.move_id,

        "move_type": chosen_candidate.move_type,

        "strategy": decision.strategy,

        "status": status,

        "rollback_reason": rollback_reason,

        "snapshot_ref": snapshot_ref,

        "x_before": current_state["vector"],

        "x_after": after_state["vector"],

        "delta_x_empirical": delta_x_empirical,

        "quality_delta": quality_delta,

        "shadow_delta": shadow_delta,

        "predicted_score": round(float(decision.final_score), 6),

        "direct_score": round(float(decision.direct_score), 6),

        "tunnel_score": round(float(decision.tunnel_score), 6),

        "efficacy": round(float(efficacy), 6),

        "corridor_ok": status == "applied",

        "notes": {

            "geom_cost": round(float(decision.notes.get("geom_cost", 0.0)), 6),

            "curvature_penalty": round(float(decision.notes.get("curvature_penalty", 0.0)), 6),

            "used_delta_x": {k: round(float(v), 6) for k, v in decision.notes.get("used_delta_x", {}).items()},

        },

        "hash_prev": prev_hash,

    }

    row_hash = witness_hash(base_row, prev_hash)

    base_row["hash"] = row_hash

    append_jsonl(paths.witness_jsonl, base_row)

    apply_witness_learning(

        witness_row=base_row,

        move_delta_memory=move_delta_memory,

        move_efficacy_memory=move_efficacy_memory,

        metric_learning_state=metric_learning_state,

        coupling_learning_state=coupling_learning_state,

        tunnel_learning_state=tunnel_learning_state,

        alpha=0.2

    )

    save_json(paths.move_delta_memory, move_delta_memory)

    save_json(paths.move_efficacy_memory, move_efficacy_memory)

    save_json(paths.metric_learning_state, metric_learning_state)

    save_json(paths.coupling_learning_state, coupling_learning_state)

    save_json(paths.tunnel_learning_state, tunnel_learning_state)

    return {

        "artifact_path": str(path),

        "adapter": adapter.name,

        "decision": asdict(decision),

        "status": status,

        "witness_hash": row_hash,

    }

# ============================================================

# DEMO DRIVER

# ============================================================

def choose_one_safe_artifact(paths: RuntimePaths) -> Optional[Tuple[Path, type[ArtifactAdapter]]]:

    artifacts = discover_artifacts(paths.artifacts_root)

    for path in artifacts:

        # avoid mutating learned memory + witness file itself in this first safe version

        if "kernel/learned" in str(path) or str(path).endswith("witness.jsonl"):

            continue

        adapter = choose_adapter(path)

        if adapter is None:

            continue

        content = adapter.load(path)

        moves = adapter.generate_candidate_moves(path, content)

        if moves:

            return path, adapter

    return None

def run_once(root: str = "athena_runtime") -> Dict[str, Any]:

    paths = build_runtime_paths(root)

    bootstrap_runtime(paths)

    seed_demo_files(paths)

    chosen = choose_one_safe_artifact(paths)

    if chosen is None:

        return {"status": "no_mutable_artifact_found"}

    path, adapter = chosen

    result = execute_one_artifact_cycle(path, adapter, paths)

    if result is None:

        return {"status": "no_candidate_move"}

    return {

        "status": "ok",

        "artifact": result["artifact_path"],

        "adapter": result["adapter"],

        "decision": result["decision"],

        "mutation_status": result["status"],

        "witness_hash": result["witness_hash"],

    }

if __name__ == "__main__":

    result = run_once("athena_runtime")

    print(json.dumps(result, indent=2))

choose one artifact with an available bounded move

extract its vector from the real file

score candidate moves with the learned kernel

snapshot the file

apply one real move

re-read the file

re-extract the empirical after-state

append a hashed witness row to witness.jsonl

update persistent learned memory JSON files

So this is the first real:

[discover \rightarrow evaluate \rightarrow mutate \rightarrow witness \rightarrow learn]

cycle on disk.

[μ₃₁₁::Square] WHY AST MATTERS

The current code adapter is text-based.That is good enough for tiny comments and docstrings, but not good enough for trustworthy code evolution.

Text edits are vulnerable to:

indentation drift

misplaced comments

docstring insertion in wrong location

accidental syntax breakage

fragile matching

So the Python adapter must become syntax-aware.

For .py files, the adapter should use:

[\texttt{ast.parse(file)}]

to inspect:

module docstring

function definitions

class definitions

function count

nesting

basic complexity proxies

safe insertion points

This upgrades the code manifold from “string surface” to “syntax surface.”

[μ₃₁₂::Cloud] AST-AWARE CODE EXTRACTION

The Python adapter should derive several measures from the AST directly.

Literal explicitness (L)

Use:

module docstring presence

function docstring coverage

class docstring coverage

argument naming sanity

Structural coherence (S)

Use:

number of top-level nodes

depth of nesting

long-function penalty

excessive branching proxy

Causal legibility (C)

Use:

import graph count

global state usage

I/O and subprocess markers

side-effect call detection

Repair accessibility (H)

Use:

number of functions

modular split

function length distribution

docstring + invariant presence

syntax validity certainty

This is far better than pure string heuristics.

[μ₃₁₃::Flower] AST-SAFE MOVE FAMILIES

Once AST is available, moves can become safer.

Safe move 1 — add module docstring

Only if:

module has no docstring

insertion point is start of file

Safe move 2 — add function docstring stub

Only if:

function lacks docstring

function body is non-empty

insertion point is first body statement

Safe move 3 — add invariant comment above first return / critical branch

Still text-based, but AST-located.

Safe move 4 — normalize overly long function with non-destructive marker

Instead of refactoring code yet, insert:

# TODO: split function

bounded witness annotation

So v0.3.2 remains conservative:it becomes AST-aware before AST-transformative.

That is the correct sequence.

[μ₃₁₄::Square] AST ADAPTER INTERFACE EXTENSION

Add Python-specific methods:

class PythonAstAdapter(CodeAdapter):

    @classmethod

    def parse_ast(cls, path: Path) -> ast.AST: ...

    

    @classmethod

    def ast_summary(cls, tree: ast.AST) -> dict: ...

    

    @classmethod

    def safe_edit_points(cls, text: str, tree: ast.AST) -> dict: ...

    

    @classmethod

    def syntax_ok(cls, text: str) -> bool: ...

This creates a higher-confidence code organ.

[μ₃₁₅::Water] AST SUMMARY MODEL

A useful AST summary object:

{

  "module_docstring": false,

  "functions": [

    {

      "name": "watch_folder",

      "lineno": 1,

      "end_lineno": 5,

      "arg_count": 1,

      "has_docstring": false,

      "body_len": 3

    }

  ],

  "classes": [],

  "imports": ["os"],

  "globals_assigned": [],

  "max_depth": 2,

  "function_count": 1,

  "class_count": 0

}

This gives the adapter a stable basis for extraction and move generation.

[μ₃₁₆::Fractal] AST-AWARE EXTRACTION LAW

For Python files, replace some string heuristics with AST-informed extractors.

Example:

[L_{py} = 0.35 \cdot module_docstring

0.35 \cdot function_docstring_coverage

0.15 \cdot naming_clarity

0.15 \cdot explicit_imports]

[S_{py} = 1 - penalty(long_functions, deep_nesting, sparse_modularity)]

[H_{py} = 1 - penalty(giant_functions, no_docstrings, no_snapshots, high_coupling)]

This makes code vectors less noisy.

[μ₃₁₉::Flower] PULSE DRIVER SELECTION STACK

The driver should use this order:

Layer 1 — read daily Pulse

Determine family focus and allowed scope.

Layer 2 — discover artifacts in allowed scope

Only consider eligible files.

Layer 3 — adapter eligibility

Choose files supported by the corresponding adapter.

Layer 4 — artifact scoring

Compute current vectors for eligible files.

Layer 5 — urgency fit

Prefer files whose weaknesses align with today’s Pulse.

Layer 6 — candidate move generation

Restrict to today’s preferred move types.

Layer 7 — navigation kernel

Choose the best lawful move.

This makes the daily system purposeful instead of opportunistic.

[μ₃₂₀::Square] ARTIFACT PRIORITIZATION UNDER PULSE

Given Pulse dimension focus (d^*), score each artifact by deficit:

[Deficit_d(X)=1-x_d(X)]

Then Pulse alignment score:

[Align(X)=w_1 \cdot Deficit_{d^*}(X)+w_2 \cdot ShadowRelevant(X)+w_3 \cdot ScopeFit(X)]

Interpretation:today’s artifact should be one that actually needs today’s kind of help.

Example:if Pulse focuses literal clarification, then prefer a code file with:

no docstring

low (L)

high ambiguity shadow

That makes the daily move coherent.

[μ₃₂₁::Cloud] PULSE-AWARE FILE CHOICE

So instead of:

pick first file with a move

do:

rank all eligible files by pulse alignment

then run the navigator on the best one or best few

This is a major improvement.

Minimal policy:

evaluate top 5 eligible artifacts

choose highest pulse-aligned artifact

then evaluate moves only inside that artifact

This stays small but smarter.

[μ₃₂₂::Water] DAILY DRIVER PSEUDOCODE

def run_daily_pulse_cycle(runtime_root):

    pulse = load_today_pulse(...)

    eligible_paths = discover_scoped_artifacts(pulse.scope)

    scored_artifacts = []

    for path in eligible_paths:

        adapter = choose_adapter(path)

        if not adapter:

            continue

        state = extract_state_for_artifact(path, adapter, witness_rows)

        align = pulse_alignment_score(state, pulse)

        scored_artifacts.append((align, path, adapter, state))

    scored_artifacts.sort(reverse=True)

    top = scored_artifacts[:5]

    best_artifact_result = None

    best_total_score = -inf

    for align, path, adapter, state in top:

        candidates = filter_moves_by_pulse(adapter.generate_candidate_moves(path, adapter.load(path)), pulse)

        decision = navigator.choose_best_move(state, candidates)

        if decision:

            total = align + decision.final_score

            if total > best_total_score:

                best_total_score = total

                best_artifact_result = (path, adapter, state, decision)

    execute(best_artifact_result)

    witness()

    learn()

That is the daily agency loop in executable form.

[μ₃₂₃::Fractal] PULSE TYPES → REAL BEHAVIOR

Prefer:

Prefer:

invariant comments

schema normalization

witness missing field repair

Prefer:

weekly summary artifacts

Prefer:

only sandbox-safe experimental files

lower confidence, higher novelty candidates

still one file only

Prefer:

collapse bloated docs to concise canonical section

not structural rewrites

This turns Pulse from abstract type into concrete repo metabolics.

[μ₃₂₄::Square] AST-SAFE CODE MOVE IMPLEMENTATION

For Python docstrings specifically:

def insert_module_docstring(text: str, doc: str) -> str:

    stripped = text.lstrip()

    if stripped.startswith('"""') or stripped.startswith("'''"):

        return text

    return f'"""{doc}"""\n\n' + text

That is the safe module case.

For function docstring insertion:

parse AST

locate first function lacking docstring

insert after function line with correct indentation

Pseudo:

def insert_function_docstring(text, fn_lineno, indent):

    lines = text.splitlines()

    idx = fn_lineno

    lines.insert(idx, f'{indent}"""Bounded function docstring."""')

    return "\n".join(lines) + "\n"

After editing:

reparse with ast.parse

if parse fails, rollback

This is the actual safety improvement.

[μ₃₂₅::Cloud] POST-EDIT VALIDATION STACK FOR PYTHON

For Python artifacts, validation should be:

file exists

UTF-8 decodes

ast.parse succeeds

corridor thresholds pass

size delta not absurd

hash changed only if move intended mutation

This means code edits are validated both:

semantically in the 12-vector corridor

syntactically in the AST corridor

That is much stronger than v0.3.1.

[μ₃₃₃::Fractal] athena_kernel_v0321.py

from __future__ import annotations

import ast

import os

import json

import math

import copy

import hashlib

from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict, field

from datetime import datetime

from pathlib import Path

from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional, Tuple

# ============================================================

# CANONICAL ORDERS

# ============================================================

VECTOR_ORDER = ["L", "S", "T", "C", "A", "N", "U", "R", "M", "P", "H", "Z"]

QUALITY_ORDER = [

    "truth", "coherence", "novelty", "utility",

    "compression", "safety", "vitality", "recoverability"

]

SHADOW_ORDER = [

    "hallucination", "fragility", "drift", "ambiguity",

    "coupling", "vanity", "noise", "loop_risk"

]

# ============================================================

# BASIC UTILS

# ============================================================

def clamp01(x: float) -> float:

    return max(0.0, min(1.0, float(x)))

def squash(x: float) -> float:

    return 1.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-x))

def mean(xs: List[float], default: float = 0.0) -> float:

    return sum(xs) / len(xs) if xs else default

def variance(xs: List[float], default: float = 0.0) -> float:

    if not xs:

        return default

    m = mean(xs)

    return sum((x - m) ** 2 for x in xs) / len(xs)

def now_iso() -> str:

    return datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z"

def ensure_dir(path: str | Path) -> None:

    Path(path).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def load_json(path: str | Path, default: Any) -> Any:

    p = Path(path)

    if not p.exists():

        return copy.deepcopy(default)

    try:

        with p.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:

            return json.load(f)

    except Exception:

        return copy.deepcopy(default)

def save_json(path: str | Path, obj: Any) -> None:

    p = Path(path)

    ensure_dir(p.parent)

    tmp = p.with_suffix(p.suffix + ".tmp")

    with tmp.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:

        json.dump(obj, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

    tmp.replace(p)

def append_jsonl(path: str | Path, row: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:

    p = Path(path)

    ensure_dir(p.parent)

    with p.open("a", encoding="utf-8") as f:

        f.write(json.dumps(row, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")

def read_jsonl(path: str | Path, limit: int = 500) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:

    p = Path(path)

    if not p.exists():

        return []

    rows: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []

    with p.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:

        for line in f:

            line = line.strip()

            if not line:

                continue

            try:

                rows.append(json.loads(line))

            except Exception:

                continue

    return rows[-limit:]

def sha256_bytes(b: bytes) -> str:

    return "sha256:" + hashlib.sha256(b).hexdigest()

def file_hash(path: str | Path) -> str:

    with open(path, "rb") as f:

        return sha256_bytes(f.read())

def add_delta(x: Dict[str, float], delta_x: Dict[str, float], lam: float = 1.0) -> Dict[str, float]:

    out = dict(x)

    for k, v in delta_x.items():

        out[k] = clamp01(float(out.get(k, 0.0)) + lam * float(v))

    return out

def vector_dict_to_list(d: Dict[str, float], order: List[str]) -> List[float]:

    return [float(d.get(k, 0.0)) for k in order]

def l2_distance_dict(a: Dict[str, float], b: Dict[str, float], order: List[str]) -> float:

    return math.sqrt(sum((float(a.get(k, 0.0)) - float(b.get(k, 0.0))) ** 2 for k in order))

def shadow_total(shadow_vector: Dict[str, float]) -> float:

    return sum(float(shadow_vector.get(k, 0.0)) for k in SHADOW_ORDER) / max(len(SHADOW_ORDER), 1)

# ============================================================

# QUALITY / SHADOW

# ============================================================

QUALITY_WEIGHTS = {

    "truth": 1.00,

    "coherence": 0.95,

    "novelty": 0.72,

    "utility": 0.90,

    "compression": 0.78,

    "safety": 1.05,

    "vitality": 0.80,

    "recoverability": 1.00,

}

SHADOW_WEIGHTS = {

    "hallucination": 1.10,

    "fragility": 1.00,

    "drift": 0.90,

    "ambiguity": 0.95,

    "coupling": 0.82,

    "vanity": 0.76,

    "noise": 0.74,

    "loop_risk": 1.02,

}

def derive_quality_vector(vector: Dict[str, float]) -> Dict[str, float]:

    novelty_raw = 0.30 * (1.0 - vector["T"]) + 0.35 * vector["A"] + 0.35 * vector["P"]

    return {

        "truth": clamp01(0.35 * vector["L"] + 0.20 * vector["U"] + 0.20 * vector["N"] + 0.25 * vector["C"]),

        "coherence": clamp01(0.45 * vector["S"] + 0.20 * vector["C"] + 0.15 * vector["A"] + 0.20 * vector["Z"]),

        "novelty": clamp01(novelty_raw),

        "utility": clamp01(0.35 * vector["L"] + 0.25 * vector["C"] + 0.20 * vector["H"] + 0.20 * vector["M"]),

        "compression": clamp01(0.65 * vector["P"] + 0.35 * vector["Z"]),

        "safety": clamp01(0.20 * vector["N"] + 0.25 * vector["U"] + 0.25 * vector["H"] + 0.30 * vector["R"]),

        "vitality": clamp01(0.30 * vector["T"] + 0.20 * vector["A"] + 0.20 * vector["M"] + 0.30 * vector["Z"]),

        "recoverability": clamp01(0.65 * vector["H"] + 0.35 * vector["Z"]),

    }

def derive_shadow_vector(vector: Dict[str, float]) -> Dict[str, float]:

    return {

        "hallucination": clamp01(1.0 - 0.6 * vector["L"] - 0.4 * vector["U"]),

        "fragility": clamp01(1.0 - 0.7 * vector["H"] - 0.3 * vector["R"]),

        "drift": clamp01(1.0 - vector["T"]),

        "ambiguity": clamp01(1.0 - 0.5 * vector["L"] - 0.5 * vector["A"]),

        "coupling": clamp01(1.0 - 0.6 * vector["C"] - 0.4 * vector["S"]),

        "vanity": clamp01(1.0 - 0.5 * vector["N"] - 0.5 * vector["U"]),

        "noise": clamp01(1.0 - 0.5 * vector["P"] - 0.5 * vector["Z"]),

        "loop_risk": clamp01(1.0 - vector["R"]),

    }

def phi_quality(q: Dict[str, float]) -> float:

    return sum(float(q[k]) * QUALITY_WEIGHTS[k] for k in QUALITY_ORDER)

def phi_shadow(s: Dict[str, float]) -> float:

    return sum(float(s[k]) * SHADOW_WEIGHTS[k] for k in SHADOW_ORDER)

def phi_net(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:

    return phi_quality(state["quality_vector"]) - phi_shadow(state["shadow_vector"])

def evaluate_vector(vector: Dict[str, float], artifact_id: str = "artifact") -> Dict[str, Any]:

    vec = {k: clamp01(float(vector.get(k, 0.0))) for k in VECTOR_ORDER}

    q = derive_quality_vector(vec)

    s = derive_shadow_vector(vec)

    return {

        "artifact_id": artifact_id,

        "vector": vec,

        "quality_vector": q,

        "shadow_vector": s,

        "invariants": {"role": "generic", "reversible": True},

    }

# ============================================================

# METRIC / CURVATURE

# ============================================================

def zeros(n: int) -> List[List[float]]:

    return [[0.0 for _ in range(n)] for _ in range(n)]

def symmetrize(M: List[List[float]]) -> List[List[float]]:

    n = len(M)

    out = zeros(n)

    for i in range(n):

        for j in range(n):

            out[i][j] = 0.5 * (M[i][j] + M[j][i])

    return out

def clamp_min_diag(M: List[List[float]], floor: float = 1e-3) -> List[List[float]]:

    out = [row[:] for row in M]

    for i in range(len(M)):

        if out[i][i] < floor:

            out[i][i] = floor

    return out

def build_metric_matrix(metric_state: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[List[float]]:

    idx = {k: i for i, k in enumerate(VECTOR_ORDER)}

    G = zeros(len(VECTOR_ORDER))

    for dim, val in metric_state.get("diagonal", {}).items():

        G[idx[dim]][idx[dim]] = float(val)

    for pair, val in metric_state.get("couplings", {}).items():

        left, right = pair.split(":")

        i, j = idx[left], idx[right]

        G[i][j] = float(val)

        G[j][i] = float(val)

    return clamp_min_diag(symmetrize(G))

def quad_form(v: List[float], G: List[List[float]]) -> float:

    total = 0.0

    n = len(v)

    for i in range(n):

        for j in range(n):

            total += v[i] * G[i][j] * v[j]

    return total

def movement_cost(delta_x: Dict[str, float], G: List[List[float]]) -> float:

    v = vector_dict_to_list(delta_x, VECTOR_ORDER)

    return math.sqrt(max(0.0, quad_form(v, G)))

def move_curvature_penalty(delta_x: Dict[str, float], K: Dict[str, Dict[str, float]]) -> float:

    dims = [k for k, v in delta_x.items() if abs(v) > 1e-12]

    total = 0.0

    for i in dims:

        for j in dims:

            if i == j:

                continue

            total += abs(float(delta_x[i]) * float(delta_x[j])) * float(K.get(i, {}).get(j, 0.0))

    return total

DEFAULT_BASE_METRIC_STATE = {

    "diagonal": {

        "L": 1.00, "S": 1.10, "T": 1.05, "C": 1.15,

        "A": 0.95, "N": 1.00, "U": 0.95, "R": 1.20,

        "M": 1.00, "P": 1.05, "H": 1.10, "Z": 1.15,

    },

    "couplings": {

        "L:S": 0.18, "S:C": 0.21, "C:H": 0.24, "N:U": 0.19,

        "R:M": 0.22, "P:Z": 0.26, "H:Z": 0.17, "T:R": 0.16, "A:M": 0.12,

    },

}

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE = {d: {e: 0.0 for e in VECTOR_ORDER} for d in VECTOR_ORDER}

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["R"]["M"] = DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["M"]["R"] = 0.40

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["C"]["H"] = DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["H"]["C"] = 0.31

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["P"]["Z"] = DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["Z"]["P"] = 0.28

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["T"]["R"] = DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["R"]["T"] = 0.25

# RUNTIME PATHS
