@dataclass

class RuntimePaths:

    root: Path

    artifacts_root: Path

    kernel_root: Path

    learned_root: Path

    witness_root: Path

    snapshots_root: Path

    config_root: Path

    pulses_daily_root: Path

    pulses_history_root: Path

    move_delta_memory: Path

    move_efficacy_memory: Path

    metric_learning_state: Path

    coupling_learning_state: Path

    tunnel_learning_state: Path

    witness_jsonl: Path

    pulse_log_jsonl: Path

    metric_prior: Path

    thresholds: Path

    tunnel_thresholds: Path

def build_runtime_paths(root: str = "athena_runtime") -> RuntimePaths:

    rp = Path(root)

    return RuntimePaths(

        root=rp,

        artifacts_root=rp / "artifacts",

        kernel_root=rp / "kernel",

        learned_root=rp / "kernel" / "learned",

        witness_root=rp / "kernel" / "witness",

        snapshots_root=rp / "kernel" / "snapshots",

        config_root=rp / "kernel" / "config",

        pulses_daily_root=rp / "kernel" / "pulses" / "daily",

        pulses_history_root=rp / "kernel" / "pulses" / "history",

        move_delta_memory=rp / "kernel" / "learned" / "move_delta_memory.json",

        move_efficacy_memory=rp / "kernel" / "learned" / "move_efficacy_memory.json",

        metric_learning_state=rp / "kernel" / "learned" / "metric_learning_state.json",

        coupling_learning_state=rp / "kernel" / "learned" / "coupling_learning_state.json",

        tunnel_learning_state=rp / "kernel" / "learned" / "tunnel_learning_state.json",

        witness_jsonl=rp / "kernel" / "witness" / "witness.jsonl",

        pulse_log_jsonl=rp / "kernel" / "pulses" / "history" / "pulse_log.jsonl",

        metric_prior=rp / "kernel" / "config" / "metric_prior.json",

        thresholds=rp / "kernel" / "config" / "thresholds.json",

        tunnel_thresholds=rp / "kernel" / "config" / "tunnel_thresholds.json",

    )

DEFAULT_THRESHOLDS = {

    "corridor": {

        "min_truth": 0.62,

        "min_safety": 0.66,

        "min_recoverability": 0.64,

        "max_shadow_total": 0.35,

    }

}

DEFAULT_TUNNEL_THRESHOLDS = {

    "min_zero_point_clarity": 0.68,

    "min_compression_quality": 0.66,

    "min_repair_accessibility": 0.62,

    "curvature_trigger": 0.12,

    "max_invariant_loss": 0.08,

}

DEFAULT_MOVE_DELTA_MEMORY = {}

DEFAULT_MOVE_EFFICACY_MEMORY = {}

DEFAULT_METRIC_LEARNING_STATE = {k: {"observed_instability": 1.0, "count": 0} for k in VECTOR_ORDER}

DEFAULT_COUPLING_LEARNING_STATE = {}

DEFAULT_TUNNEL_LEARNING_STATE = {"global": {"count": 0, "mean_tunnel_advantage": 0.0}}

def today_pulse_filename() -> str:

    return f"pulse_{datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y_%m_%d')}.json"

def default_today_pulse(paths: RuntimePaths) -> Dict[str, Any]:

    return {

        "pulse_id": f"pulse_{datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y_%m_%d')}",

        "date": datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y-%m-%d"),

        "pulse_type": "clarification_pulse",

        "artifact_family_focus": "code",

        "scope": {

            "allowed_roots": [str(paths.artifacts_root / "code")],

            "max_files": 1,

            "deny_patterns": ["kernel/learned", "kernel/witness", "kernel/pulses/history"]

        },

        "preferred_move_types": ["code_clarify", "code_repair"],

        "selection_bias": {

            "dimension_focus": 1,

            "lens": "square",

            "change_mode": "Sa"

        },

        "shadow_warning": "avoid structural rewrites; syntax preservation required",

        "success_signal": "one bounded clarity gain with valid parse",

        "meta_observer_check": True

    }

def bootstrap_runtime(paths: RuntimePaths) -> None:

    for p in [

        paths.artifacts_root / "code",

        paths.artifacts_root / "manuscripts",

        paths.artifacts_root / "witness",

        paths.artifacts_root / "state",

        paths.learned_root,

        paths.witness_root,

        paths.snapshots_root,

        paths.config_root,

        paths.pulses_daily_root,

        paths.pulses_history_root,

    ]:

        ensure_dir(p)

    if not paths.metric_prior.exists():

        save_json(paths.metric_prior, DEFAULT_BASE_METRIC_STATE)

    if not paths.thresholds.exists():

        save_json(paths.thresholds, DEFAULT_THRESHOLDS)

    if not paths.tunnel_thresholds.exists():

        save_json(paths.tunnel_thresholds, DEFAULT_TUNNEL_THRESHOLDS)

    if not paths.move_delta_memory.exists():

        save_json(paths.move_delta_memory, DEFAULT_MOVE_DELTA_MEMORY)

    if not paths.move_efficacy_memory.exists():

        save_json(paths.move_efficacy_memory, DEFAULT_MOVE_EFFICACY_MEMORY)

    if not paths.metric_learning_state.exists():

        save_json(paths.metric_learning_state, DEFAULT_METRIC_LEARNING_STATE)

    if not paths.coupling_learning_state.exists():

        save_json(paths.coupling_learning_state, DEFAULT_COUPLING_LEARNING_STATE)

    if not paths.tunnel_learning_state.exists():

        save_json(paths.tunnel_learning_state, DEFAULT_TUNNEL_LEARNING_STATE)

    pulse_path = paths.pulses_daily_root / today_pulse_filename()

    if not pulse_path.exists():

        save_json(pulse_path, default_today_pulse(paths))

def seed_demo_files(paths: RuntimePaths) -> None:

    code_file = paths.artifacts_root / "code" / "gateway_demo.py"

    md_file = paths.artifacts_root / "manuscripts" / "chapter_demo.md"

    if not code_file.exists():

        code_file.write_text(

            "import os\n\n"

            "def watch_folder(path):\n"

            "    files = []\n"

            "    for name in os.listdir(path):\n"

            "        files.append(name)\n"

            "    return files\n",

            encoding="utf-8"

        )

    if not md_file.exists():

        md_file.write_text(

            "# Demo Chapter\n\n"

            "This section discusses the corridor process.\n\n"

            "The corridor matters.\n",

            encoding="utf-8"

        )

# ============================================================

# ADAPTERS

# ============================================================

class ArtifactAdapter:

    name = "base"

    @classmethod

    def can_handle(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        return False

    @classmethod

    def load(cls, path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        raise NotImplementedError

    @classmethod

    def extract_vector(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any], history: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        raise NotImplementedError

    @classmethod

    def generate_candidate_moves(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any]) -> List["CandidateMove"]:

        return []

    @classmethod

    def apply_move(cls, path: Path, move: "CandidateMove") -> Dict[str, Any]:

        raise NotImplementedError

    @classmethod

    def basic_parse_ok(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        try:

            cls.load(path)

            return True

        except Exception:

            return False

    @classmethod

    def snapshot(cls, path: Path, snapshot_root: Path) -> str:

        ts = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H-%M-%SZ")

        ensure_dir(snapshot_root / ts)

        safe_name = str(path).replace("/", "__").replace("\\", "__")

        snap = snapshot_root / ts / f"{safe_name}.bak"

        with open(path, "rb") as src, open(snap, "wb") as dst:

            dst.write(src.read())

        return str(snap)

    @classmethod

    def restore_snapshot(cls, snapshot_ref: str, path: Path) -> None:

        with open(snapshot_ref, "rb") as src, open(path, "wb") as dst:

            dst.write(src.read())

class PythonAstAdapter(ArtifactAdapter):

    name = "code"

    @classmethod

    def can_handle(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        return path.suffix.lower() == ".py"

    @classmethod

    def parse_ast(cls, path: Path) -> ast.AST:

        text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

        return ast.parse(text)

    @classmethod

    def ast_summary(cls, tree: ast.AST) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        functions = []

        classes = []

        imports = []

        globals_assigned = []

        max_depth = 0

        class DepthVisitor(ast.NodeVisitor):

            def __init__(self) -> None:

                self.depth = 0

                self.max_depth = 0

            def generic_visit(self, node):

                self.depth += 1

                self.max_depth = max(self.max_depth, self.depth)

                super().generic_visit(node)

                self.depth -= 1

        dv = DepthVisitor()

        dv.visit(tree)

        max_depth = dv.max_depth

        for node in ast.walk(tree):

            if isinstance(node, (ast.Import, ast.ImportFrom)):

                if isinstance(node, ast.Import):

                    imports.extend(alias.name for alias in node.names)

                else:

                    imports.append(node.module or "")

            elif isinstance(node, ast.FunctionDef):

                functions.append({

                    "name": node.name,

                    "lineno": getattr(node, "lineno", 1),

                    "end_lineno": getattr(node, "end_lineno", getattr(node, "lineno", 1)),

                    "arg_count": len(node.args.args),

                    "has_docstring": ast.get_docstring(node) is not None,

                    "body_len": len(node.body),

                })

            elif isinstance(node, ast.ClassDef):

                classes.append({

                    "name": node.name,

                    "lineno": getattr(node, "lineno", 1),

                    "end_lineno": getattr(node, "end_lineno", getattr(node, "lineno", 1)),

                    "has_docstring": ast.get_docstring(node) is not None,

                    "body_len": len(node.body),

                })

            elif isinstance(node, ast.Assign):

                for tgt in node.targets:

                    if isinstance(tgt, ast.Name):

                        globals_assigned.append(tgt.id)

        return {

            "module_docstring": ast.get_docstring(tree) is not None,

            "functions": functions,

            "classes": classes,

            "imports": imports,

            "globals_assigned": globals_assigned,

            "max_depth": max_depth,

            "function_count": len(functions),

            "class_count": len(classes),

        }

    @classmethod

    def load(cls, path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

        tree = ast.parse(text)

        summary = cls.ast_summary(tree)

        lines = text.splitlines()

        return {

            "text": text,

            "lines": lines,

            "line_count": len(lines),

            "tree": tree,

            "summary": summary,

        }

    @classmethod

    def syntax_ok(cls, text: str) -> bool:

        try:

            ast.parse(text)

            return True

        except Exception:

            return False

    @classmethod

    def extract_vector(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any], history: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        s = content["summary"]

        line_count = max(1, content["line_count"])

        fn_count = s["function_count"]

        class_count = s["class_count"]

        fn_docs = mean([1.0 if f["has_docstring"] else 0.0 for f in s["functions"]], default=0.0)

        class_docs = mean([1.0 if c["has_docstring"] else 0.0 for c in s["classes"]], default=0.0)

        module_doc = 1.0 if s["module_docstring"] else 0.0

        doc_cov = 0.5 * module_doc + 0.35 * fn_docs + 0.15 * class_docs

        long_fn_penalty = sum(1 for f in s["functions"] if (f["end_lineno"] - f["lineno"]) > 25) * 0.12

        deep_penalty = max(0.0, (s["max_depth"] - 6) * 0.04)

        sparse_modularity = 0.18 if line_count > 180 and fn_count <= 1 else 0.0

        import_count = len(s["imports"])

        global_count = len(s["globals_assigned"])

        subprocess_penalty = 1.0 if "subprocess" in s["imports"] else 0.0

        role_scores = {

            "bridge": 0.75 if any("watch" in f["name"] or "copy" in f["name"] for f in s["functions"]) else 0.35,

            "witness": 0.70 if "hashlib" in s["imports"] or "json" in s["imports"] else 0.30,

            "guard": 0.60 if any("validate" in f["name"] for f in s["functions"]) else 0.25,

        }

        role_confusion_penalty = 0.05 if len([v for v in role_scores.values() if v > 0.6]) > 2 else 0.0

        identified_failure_modes = int(any("except" in line for line in content["lines"])) + int(any("if " in line for line in content["lines"]))

        expected_failure_modes = 3

        shadow_blindness_penalty = 0.12 if identified_failure_modes == 0 else 0.03

        claimed_confidence = 0.78 if module_doc else 0.52

        support_confidence = 0.55 + 0.20 * fn_docs + 0.10 * class_docs

        degradation_under_iteration = 0.12 if long_fn_penalty > 0 else 0.04

        loop_blowup = 0.12 if any("while True" in line for line in content["lines"]) and "seen" not in content["text"] else 0.03

        agent_scores = [0.66, 0.73, 0.61, 0.69]

        compression_fidelity = 0.78 if fn_count <= 5 else 0.56

        compression_compactness = 0.70 if line_count < 150 else 0.45

        compression_lossy_risk = 0.14 if long_fn_penalty > 0 else 0.06

        repair_cost = clamp01(0.10 + 0.0025 * line_count + 0.04 * global_count)

        rollback_difficulty = 0.08

        irreversibility = 0.05

        seed_clarity = 0.76 if module_doc else 0.55

        invariant_preservation = 0.72 if any("# invariant:" in line.lower() for line in content["lines"]) else 0.55

        collapse_distortion = 0.12 if line_count > 220 else 0.05

        vector = {

            "L": clamp01(doc_cov),

            "S": clamp01(1.0 - long_fn_penalty - deep_penalty - sparse_modularity),

            "T": clamp01(squash(3.0 * ((0.18 if history else 0.0) - 0.0 - (0.08 if line_count > 180 else 0.03)))),

            "C": clamp01(1.0 - max(0, import_count - 5) * 0.08 - global_count * 0.10 - subprocess_penalty * 0.12),

            "A": clamp01(max(role_scores.values()) - role_confusion_penalty),

            "N": clamp01((identified_failure_modes / expected_failure_modes) - shadow_blindness_penalty),

            "U": clamp01(1.0 - abs(claimed_confidence - support_confidence)),

            "R": clamp01(1.0 - 0.6 * degradation_under_iteration - 0.8 * loop_blowup),

            "M": clamp01(mean(agent_scores) - 0.5 * variance(agent_scores)),

            "P": clamp01(0.45 * compression_fidelity + 0.35 * compression_compactness - 0.30 * compression_lossy_risk),

            "H": clamp01(1.0 - (0.45 * repair_cost + 0.35 * rollback_difficulty + 0.45 * irreversibility)),

            "Z": clamp01(0.45 * seed_clarity + 0.40 * invariant_preservation - 0.40 * collapse_distortion),

        }

        return {

            "artifact_id": str(path.relative_to(path.parents[1])),

            "artifact_type": cls.name,

            "path": str(path),

            "vector": vector,

            "quality_vector": derive_quality_vector(vector),

            "shadow_vector": derive_shadow_vector(vector),

            "invariants": {"role": "code", "reversible": True},

        }

    @classmethod

    def generate_candidate_moves(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any]) -> List["CandidateMove"]:

        s = content["summary"]

        moves: List[CandidateMove] = []

        if not s["module_docstring"]:

            moves.append(CandidateMove(

                move_id="code_add_module_docstring",

                title="Add bounded module docstring",

                move_type="code_clarify",

                delta_x={"L": 0.08, "S": 0.02, "P": 0.02, "H": 0.01},

                drift_risk=0.01,

                repetition_penalty=0.00,

                seed_gain=0.04,

                curvature_penalty_hint=0.02,

                target_template="default_template",

            ))

        first_undoc_fn = next((f for f in s["functions"] if not f["has_docstring"] and f["body_len"] > 0), None)

        if first_undoc_fn:

            moves.append(CandidateMove(

                move_id="code_add_function_docstring",

                title="Add bounded function docstring",

                move_type="code_clarify",

                delta_x={"L": 0.06, "S": 0.01, "H": 0.02, "A": 0.01},

                drift_risk=0.02,

                repetition_penalty=0.01,

                seed_gain=0.05,

                curvature_penalty_hint=0.03,

                target_template="default_template",

            ))

        if s["functions"] and "# invariant:" not in content["text"].lower():

            moves.append(CandidateMove(

                move_id="code_add_invariant_comment",

                title="Add one bounded invariant comment",

                move_type="code_repair",

                delta_x={"H": 0.06, "Z": 0.03, "L": 0.03, "N": 0.01},

                drift_risk=0.02,

                repetition_penalty=0.01,

                seed_gain=0.06,

                curvature_penalty_hint=0.03,

                target_template="repair_template",

            ))

        return moves

    @classmethod

    def apply_move(cls, path: Path, move: "CandidateMove") -> Dict[str, Any]:

        text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

        if move.move_id == "code_add_module_docstring":

            stripped = text.lstrip()

            if not (stripped.startswith('"""') or stripped.startswith("'''")):

                text = '"""Athena managed: bounded module docstring."""\n\n' + text

        elif move.move_id == "code_add_function_docstring":

            tree = ast.parse(text)

            target = None

            for node in ast.walk(tree):

                if isinstance(node, ast.FunctionDef) and ast.get_docstring(node) is None and node.body:

                    target = node

                    break

            if target is not None:

                lines = text.splitlines()

                insert_at = int(target.lineno)

                fn_line = lines[target.lineno - 1]

                indent = " " * (len(fn_line) - len(fn_line.lstrip()) + 4)

                lines.insert(insert_at, f'{indent}"""Bounded function docstring."""')

                text = "\n".join(lines) + ("\n" if not text.endswith("\n") else "")

                ast.parse(text)

        elif move.move_id == "code_add_invariant_comment":

            tree = ast.parse(text)

            target = None

            for node in ast.walk(tree):

                if isinstance(node, ast.FunctionDef):

                    target = node

                    break

            if target is not None:

                lines = text.splitlines()

                insert_at = int(target.lineno)

                fn_line = lines[target.lineno - 1]

                indent = " " * (len(fn_line) - len(fn_line.lstrip()) + 4)

                lines.insert(insert_at, f"{indent}# invariant: preserve bounded reversible behavior")

                text = "\n".join(lines) + ("\n" if not text.endswith("\n") else "")

                ast.parse(text)

        path.write_text(text, encoding="utf-8")

        return {"status": "ok", "move_id": move.move_id}

    @classmethod

    def basic_parse_ok(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        try:

            text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

            ast.parse(text)

            return True

        except Exception:

            return False

class MarkdownAdapter(ArtifactAdapter):

    name = "manuscript"

    @classmethod

    def can_handle(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        return path.suffix.lower() in {".md", ".txt"}

    @classmethod

    def load(cls, path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

        lines = text.splitlines()

        headings = [ln for ln in lines if ln.strip().startswith("#")]

        return {

            "text": text,

            "lines": lines,

            "line_count": len(lines),

            "headings": headings,

            "paragraphs": [p for p in text.split("\n\n") if p.strip()],

        }

    @classmethod

    def extract_vector(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any], history: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        text = content["text"]

        heading_count = len(content["headings"])

        para_count = len(content["paragraphs"])

        line_count = max(1, content["line_count"])

        explicit_fields_present = 1 if heading_count > 0 else 0

        explicit_fields_expected = 1

        ambiguous_labels = text.lower().count("something") + text.lower().count("stuff")

        undefined_refs = text.lower().count("it") if len(text) < 100 else max(0, text.lower().count("it") - 3)

        duplication = max(0, para_count - len(set(p.strip() for p in content["paragraphs"])))

        orphan_nodes = 1 if heading_count == 0 else 0

        invalid_nesting = 1 if any(h.count("#") > 4 for h in content["headings"]) else 0

        vector = {

            "L": clamp01((explicit_fields_present / explicit_fields_expected) - 0.05 * ambiguous_labels - 0.05 * undefined_refs),

            "S": clamp01(1.0 - 0.10 * duplication - 0.18 * orphan_nodes - 0.10 * invalid_nesting),

            "T": clamp01(squash(3.0 * ((0.15 if history else 0.0) - 0.0 - (0.07 if line_count > 180 else 0.03)))),

            "C": clamp01(1.0 - (0.12 if ("corridor" in text.lower() and "definition" not in text.lower()) else 0.0)),

            "A": 0.68 if heading_count > 0 else 0.45,

            "N": 0.70 if ("warning" in text.lower() or "avoid" in text.lower()) else 0.45,

            "U": 0.72 if heading_count > 0 else 0.56,

            "R": 0.70 if text.lower().count("next") < 6 else 0.55,

            "M": 0.66,

            "P": 0.76 if para_count <= 8 else 0.58,

            "H": 0.80 if line_count < 160 else 0.68,

            "Z": 0.74 if "summary" in text.lower() else 0.58,

        }

        return {

            "artifact_id": str(path.relative_to(path.parents[1])),

            "artifact_type": cls.name,

            "path": str(path),

            "vector": vector,

            "quality_vector": derive_quality_vector(vector),

            "shadow_vector": derive_shadow_vector(vector),

            "invariants": {"role": "manuscript", "reversible": True},

        }

    @classmethod

    def generate_candidate_moves(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any]) -> List["CandidateMove"]:

        moves: List[CandidateMove] = []

        text = content["text"]

        if "Definition:" not in text and "corridor" in text.lower():

            moves.append(CandidateMove(

                move_id="md_add_definition",

                title="Add one bounded definition line",

                move_type="manuscript_clarify",

                delta_x={"L": 0.08, "U": 0.05, "A": 0.02, "N": 0.01},

                drift_risk=0.01,

                repetition_penalty=0.00,

                seed_gain=0.04,

                curvature_penalty_hint=0.02,

            ))

        if "## Seed Summary" not in text:

            moves.append(CandidateMove(

                move_id="md_add_seed_summary",

                title="Add one bounded seed summary section",

                move_type="manuscript_compress",

                delta_x={"P": 0.06, "Z": 0.04, "L": 0.03},

                drift_risk=0.015,

                repetition_penalty=0.01,

                seed_gain=0.07,

                curvature_penalty_hint=0.03,

                target_template="compression_template",

            ))

        return moves

    @classmethod

    def apply_move(cls, path: Path, move: "CandidateMove") -> Dict[str, Any]:

        text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

        if move.move_id == "md_add_definition" and "Definition:" not in text:

            insertion = "\nDefinition: Corridor = the bounded safe operating region for changes.\n"

            parts = text.splitlines()

            if parts and parts[0].startswith("#"):

                parts.insert(1, insertion.strip("\n"))

                text = "\n".join(parts) + "\n"

            else:

                text += insertion

        elif move.move_id == "md_add_seed_summary" and "## Seed Summary" not in text:

            text = text.rstrip() + "\n\n## Seed Summary\n\n- Core idea collapsed into bounded form.\n"

        path.write_text(text, encoding="utf-8")

        return {"status": "ok", "move_id": move.move_id}

class WitnessAdapter(ArtifactAdapter):

    name = "witness"

    @classmethod

    def can_handle(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        return path.suffix.lower() == ".jsonl"

    @classmethod

    def load(cls, path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        rows = read_jsonl(path, limit=200)

        return {"rows": rows, "count": len(rows)}

    @classmethod

    def extract_vector(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any], history: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        rows = content["rows"]

        required = ["move_id", "strategy", "x_before", "x_after", "efficacy"]

        explicit = 0.0

        if rows:

            explicit = sum(1 for k in required if k in rows[-1]) / len(required)

        vector = {

            "L": explicit,

            "S": 0.90 if all(isinstance(r, dict) for r in rows[-10:]) else 0.50,

            "T": 0.60,

            "C": 0.70,

            "A": 0.62,

            "N": 0.75 if rows else 0.40,

            "U": 0.78,

            "R": 0.70,

            "M": 0.60,

            "P": clamp01(0.50 + min(0.25, len(rows) * 0.01)),

            "H": 0.72,

            "Z": clamp01(0.50 + min(0.20, len(rows) * 0.008)),

        }

        return {

            "artifact_id": str(path.relative_to(path.parents[1])),

            "artifact_type": cls.name,

            "path": str(path),

            "vector": vector,

            "quality_vector": derive_quality_vector(vector),

            "shadow_vector": derive_shadow_vector(vector),

            "invariants": {"role": "witness", "reversible": True},

        }

class StateAdapter(ArtifactAdapter):

    name = "state"

    @classmethod

    def can_handle(cls, path: Path) -> bool:

        return path.suffix.lower() in {".json", ".yaml", ".yml"} and "learned" not in str(path)

    @classmethod

    def load(cls, path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        if path.suffix.lower() == ".json":

            return load_json(path, {})

        return {"raw_text": path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")}

    @classmethod

    def extract_vector(cls, path: Path, content: Dict[str, Any], history: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

        keys = list(content.keys()) if isinstance(content, dict) else []

        vector = {

            "L": clamp01(0.55 + 0.02 * len(keys)),

            "S": 0.72 if isinstance(content, dict) else 0.45,

            "T": 0.58, "C": 0.62, "A": 0.60, "N": 0.55,

            "U": 0.66, "R": 0.61, "M": 0.58, "P": 0.65, "H": 0.70, "Z": 0.64,

        }

        return {

            "artifact_id": str(path.relative_to(path.parents[1])),

            "artifact_type": cls.name,

            "path": str(path),

            "vector": vector,

            "quality_vector": derive_quality_vector(vector),

            "shadow_vector": derive_shadow_vector(vector),

            "invariants": {"role": "state", "reversible": True},

        }

ADAPTERS = [WitnessAdapter, StateAdapter, PythonAstAdapter, MarkdownAdapter]

def choose_adapter(path: Path) -> Optional[type[ArtifactAdapter]]:

    for adapter in ADAPTERS:

        if adapter.can_handle(path):

            return adapter

    return None

# ============================================================

# CANDIDATE / DECISION

# ============================================================

@dataclass

class CandidateMove:

    move_id: str

    title: str

    move_type: str

    delta_x: Dict[str, float]

    drift_risk: float

    repetition_penalty: float

    seed_gain: float

    curvature_penalty_hint: float = 0.0

    target_template: str = "default_template"

    reversible: bool = True

    corridor_safe_hint: bool = True

@dataclass

class KernelDecision:

    move_id: str

    title: str

    strategy: str

    direct_score: float

    tunnel_score: float

    final_score: float

    projected_lambda: float

    notes: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)

# ============================================================

# LEARNING MEMORY

# ============================================================

def blended_delta_x(candidate_delta_x, move_memory_entry, kappa0=5.0):

    if not move_memory_entry:

        return dict(candidate_delta_x)

    count = float(move_memory_entry.get("count", 0))

    mean_dx = move_memory_entry.get("mean_delta_x", {})

    var_dx = move_memory_entry.get("variance_delta_x", {})

    avg_var = sum(float(var_dx.get(k, 0.0)) for k in VECTOR_ORDER) / len(VECTOR_ORDER)

    conf = (count / (count + kappa0)) * (1.0 / (1.0 + avg_var))

    out = {}

    for k in VECTOR_ORDER:

        templ = float(candidate_delta_x.get(k, 0.0))

        learned = float(mean_dx.get(k, templ))

        out[k] = (1 - conf) * templ + conf * learned

    return out

def efficacy_prior_bonus(move_id: str, move_efficacy_memory: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[float, float]:

    entry = move_efficacy_memory.get(move_id)

    if not entry:

        return 0.0, 0.0

    return float(entry.get("mean_efficacy", 0.0)), float(entry.get("variance_efficacy", 0.0))

def tunnel_advantage_prior(move_id: str, tunnel_learning_state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:

    entry = tunnel_learning_state.get(move_id)

    if not entry:

        return float(tunnel_learning_state.get("global", {}).get("mean_tunnel_advantage", 0.0))

    return float(entry.get("mean_tunnel_advantage", 0.0))

def build_learned_metric_state(

    base_metric_state: Dict[str, Any],

    metric_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

    coupling_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

    eta_diag: float = 0.35,

    eta_coup: float = 0.45

) -> Dict[str, Any]:

    out = {

        "diagonal": dict(base_metric_state.get("diagonal", {})),

        "couplings": dict(base_metric_state.get("couplings", {})),

    }

    for dim in VECTOR_ORDER:

        base = float(out["diagonal"].get(dim, 1.0))

        learned = float(metric_learning_state.get(dim, {}).get("observed_instability", base))

        out["diagonal"][dim] = max(1e-3, (1 - eta_diag) * base + eta_diag * learned)

    for pair, entry in coupling_learning_state.items():

        base = float(out["couplings"].get(pair, 0.0))

        learned = float(entry.get("observed_coupling", base))

        out["couplings"][pair] = (1 - eta_coup) * base + eta_coup * learned

    return out

def build_learned_curvature_state(base_curvature_state, tunnel_learning_state):

    return copy.deepcopy(base_curvature_state)

def update_move_delta_memory(memory, move_id, delta_x_empirical, alpha=0.2):

    entry = memory.setdefault(move_id, {

        "count": 0,

        "mean_delta_x": {k: 0.0 for k in VECTOR_ORDER},

        "variance_delta_x": {k: 0.0 for k in VECTOR_ORDER},

    })

    entry["count"] += 1

    for k in VECTOR_ORDER:

        old_mean = float(entry["mean_delta_x"][k])

        x = float(delta_x_empirical.get(k, 0.0))

        new_mean = (1 - alpha) * old_mean + alpha * x

        old_var = float(entry["variance_delta_x"][k])

        new_var = (1 - alpha) * old_var + alpha * (x - new_mean) ** 2

        entry["mean_delta_x"][k] = new_mean

        entry["variance_delta_x"][k] = new_var

def update_move_efficacy_memory(memory, move_id, strategy, efficacy, corridor_ok, alpha=0.2):

    entry = memory.setdefault(move_id, {

        "count": 0,

        "mean_efficacy": 0.0,

        "variance_efficacy": 0.0,

        "corridor_success_rate": 1.0,

        "strategy_breakdown": {}

    })

    entry["count"] += 1

    old_mean = float(entry["mean_efficacy"])

    new_mean = (1 - alpha) * old_mean + alpha * efficacy

    old_var = float(entry["variance_efficacy"])

    new_var = (1 - alpha) * old_var + alpha * (efficacy - new_mean) ** 2

    old_corr = float(entry["corridor_success_rate"])

    new_corr = (1 - alpha) * old_corr + alpha * (1.0 if corridor_ok else 0.0)

    entry["mean_efficacy"] = new_mean

    entry["variance_efficacy"] = new_var

    entry["corridor_success_rate"] = new_corr

    strat = entry["strategy_breakdown"].setdefault(strategy, {"count": 0, "mean_efficacy": 0.0})

    strat["count"] += 1

    strat["mean_efficacy"] = (1 - alpha) * float(strat["mean_efficacy"]) + alpha * efficacy

def update_metric_learning_state(metric_learning, delta_x_empirical, shadow_delta, alpha=0.2):

    shadow_up = sum(max(float(v), 0.0) for v in shadow_delta.values())

    for k in VECTOR_ORDER:

        entry = metric_learning.setdefault(k, {"observed_instability": 1.0, "count": 0})

        entry["count"] += 1

        signal = abs(float(delta_x_empirical.get(k, 0.0))) * (1.0 + shadow_up)

        old = float(entry["observed_instability"])

        entry["observed_instability"] = (1 - alpha) * old + alpha * max(1e-3, signal)

def update_coupling_learning_state(coupling_learning, delta_x_empirical, shadow_delta, alpha=0.2):

    shadow_up = sum(max(float(v), 0.0) for v in shadow_delta.values())

    for i_idx, i in enumerate(VECTOR_ORDER):

        for j in VECTOR_ORDER[i_idx + 1:]:

            pair = f"{i}:{j}"

            entry = coupling_learning.setdefault(pair, {"observed_coupling": 0.0, "count": 0})

            entry["count"] += 1

            signal = abs(float(delta_x_empirical.get(i, 0.0)) * float(delta_x_empirical.get(j, 0.0))) * (1.0 + shadow_up)

            old = float(entry["observed_coupling"])

            entry["observed_coupling"] = (1 - alpha) * old + alpha * signal

def update_tunnel_learning_state(tunnel_learning, move_id, strategy, direct_score, tunnel_score_val, efficacy, alpha=0.2):

    global_entry = tunnel_learning.setdefault("global", {"count": 0, "mean_tunnel_advantage": 0.0})

    move_entry = tunnel_learning.setdefault(move_id, {"count": 0, "mean_tunnel_advantage": 0.0, "tunnel_success_rate": 0.5})

    adv = float(tunnel_score_val) - float(direct_score)

    for entry in (global_entry, move_entry):

        entry["count"] += 1

        old = float(entry["mean_tunnel_advantage"])

        entry["mean_tunnel_advantage"] = (1 - alpha) * old + alpha * adv

    if strategy == "tunnel":

        old_sr = float(move_entry["tunnel_success_rate"])

        move_entry["tunnel_success_rate"] = (1 - alpha) * old_sr + alpha * (1.0 if efficacy > 0 else 0.0)

def apply_witness_learning(

    witness_row,

    move_delta_memory,

    move_efficacy_memory,

    metric_learning_state,

    coupling_learning_state,

    tunnel_learning_state,

    alpha=0.2

):

    update_move_delta_memory(move_delta_memory, witness_row["move_id"], witness_row["delta_x_empirical"], alpha=alpha)

    update_move_efficacy_memory(move_efficacy_memory, witness_row["move_id"], witness_row["strategy"], float(witness_row["efficacy"]), bool(witness_row["corridor_ok"]), alpha=alpha)

    update_metric_learning_state(metric_learning_state, witness_row["delta_x_empirical"], witness_row["shadow_delta"], alpha=alpha)

    update_coupling_learning_state(coupling_learning_state, witness_row["delta_x_empirical"], witness_row["shadow_delta"], alpha=alpha)

    update_tunnel_learning_state(tunnel_learning_state, witness_row["move_id"], witness_row["strategy"], float(witness_row["direct_score"]), float(witness_row["tunnel_score"]), float(witness_row["efficacy"]), alpha=alpha)

# ============================================================

# DISCOVERY / PULSE

# ============================================================

def discover_artifacts(root: str | Path) -> List[Path]:

    allowed_ext = {".py", ".md", ".txt", ".json", ".jsonl", ".yaml", ".yml"}

    out: List[Path] = []

    for dirpath, _dirnames, filenames in os.walk(root):

        for fn in filenames:

            p = Path(dirpath) / fn

            if p.suffix.lower() in allowed_ext:

                out.append(p)

    return sorted(out)

def load_today_pulse(paths: RuntimePaths) -> Dict[str, Any]:

    return load_json(paths.pulses_daily_root / today_pulse_filename(), default_today_pulse(paths))

def discover_scoped_artifacts(pulse: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Path]:

    roots = [Path(r) for r in pulse.get("scope", {}).get("allowed_roots", [])]

    deny_patterns = pulse.get("scope", {}).get("deny_patterns", [])

    out: List[Path] = []

    for root in roots:

        for path in discover_artifacts(root):

            sp = str(path)

            if any(dp in sp for dp in deny_patterns):

                continue

            out.append(path)

    return sorted(out)

def filter_moves_by_pulse(candidates: List[CandidateMove], pulse: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[CandidateMove]:

    preferred = set(pulse.get("preferred_move_types", []))

    if not preferred:

        return candidates

    filtered = [c for c in candidates if c.move_type in preferred]

    return filtered if filtered else candidates

def pulse_alignment_score(state: Dict[str, Any], pulse: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:

    dim_focus = int(pulse.get("selection_bias", {}).get("dimension_focus", 1))

    key = VECTOR_ORDER[max(0, min(len(VECTOR_ORDER) - 1, dim_focus - 1))]

    deficit = 1.0 - float(state["vector"].get(key, 0.5))

    fam = pulse.get("artifact_family_focus", "")

    fam_match = 1.0 if state.get("artifact_type") == fam or (fam == "code" and state.get("artifact_type") == "code") else 0.0

    shadow_rel = 0.0

    if key == "L":

        shadow_rel = float(state["shadow_vector"].get("ambiguity", 0.0))

    elif key == "H":

        shadow_rel = float(state["shadow_vector"].get("fragility", 0.0))

    elif key == "P":

        shadow_rel = float(state["shadow_vector"].get("noise", 0.0))

    elif key == "R":

        shadow_rel = float(state["shadow_vector"].get("loop_risk", 0.0))

    else:

        shadow_rel = shadow_total(state["shadow_vector"])

    return 0.55 * deficit + 0.25 * shadow_rel + 0.20 * fam_match

# ============================================================

# NAVIGATOR

# ============================================================

def inside_corridor(candidate_state: Dict[str, Any], thresholds: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:

    q = candidate_state["quality_vector"]

    s = candidate_state["shadow_vector"]

    c = thresholds["corridor"]

    return (

        float(q["truth"]) >= float(c["min_truth"]) and

        float(q["safety"]) >= float(c["min_safety"]) and

        float(q["recoverability"]) >= float(c["min_recoverability"]) and

        shadow_total(s) <= float(c["max_shadow_total"])

    )

def shrink_back_projection(

    x: Dict[str, float],

    delta_x: Dict[str, float],

    evaluator,

    thresholds: Dict[str, Any],

    steps: int,

    artifact_id: str

) -> Optional[Tuple[float, Dict[str, Any]]]:

    for n in range(steps, -1, -1):

        lam = n / max(steps, 1)

        candidate_vec = add_delta(x, delta_x, lam)

        candidate_state = evaluator(candidate_vec, artifact_id=artifact_id)

        if inside_corridor(candidate_state, thresholds):

            return lam, candidate_state

    return None

def should_tunnel(candidate: CandidateMove, current_state: Dict[str, Any], tunnel_thresholds: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:

    v = current_state["vector"]

    return (

        float(candidate.curvature_penalty_hint) >= float(tunnel_thresholds["curvature_trigger"]) and

        float(v["Z"]) >= float(tunnel_thresholds["min_zero_point_clarity"]) and

        float(v["P"]) >= float(tunnel_thresholds["min_compression_quality"]) and

        float(v["H"]) >= float(tunnel_thresholds["min_repair_accessibility"])

    )

def collapse_to_seed(current_state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

    vec = current_state["vector"]

    return {

        "seed_id": f"{current_state.get('artifact_id', 'artifact')}_seed",

        "compressed_vector": {"L": vec["L"], "S": vec["S"], "C": vec["C"], "P": vec["P"], "H": vec["H"], "Z": vec["Z"]},

    }

def expand_from_seed(seed: Dict[str, Any], target_template: str = "default_template") -> Dict[str, float]:

    base = {k: 0.5 for k in VECTOR_ORDER}

    for k, v in seed.get("compressed_vector", {}).items():

        base[k] = clamp01(v)

    if target_template == "repair_template":

        base["H"] = clamp01(base["H"] + 0.05)

        base["Z"] = clamp01(base["Z"] + 0.03)

        base["N"] = clamp01(base["N"] + 0.02)

    elif target_template == "compression_template":

        base["P"] = clamp01(base["P"] + 0.05)

        base["Z"] = clamp01(base["Z"] + 0.03)

    elif target_template == "event_bus_bridge_template":

        base["S"] = clamp01(base["S"] + 0.04)

        base["C"] = clamp01(base["C"] + 0.03)

        base["R"] = clamp01(base["R"] - 0.01)

        base["M"] = clamp01(base["M"] + 0.02)

    return base

def invariant_loss_penalty(seed: Dict[str, Any], expanded_vector: Dict[str, float]) -> float:

    comp = seed.get("compressed_vector", {})

    if not comp:

        return 0.0

    total = 0.0

    for k, v in comp.items():

        total += abs(float(v) - float(expanded_vector.get(k, 0.0)))

    return total / len(comp)

def tunnel_score(current_state: Dict[str, Any], candidate: CandidateMove, evaluator) -> Tuple[float, Dict[str, Any]]:

    seed = collapse_to_seed(current_state)

    expanded_vec = expand_from_seed(seed, candidate.target_template)

    expanded_state = evaluator(expanded_vec, artifact_id=current_state["artifact_id"])

    current_q = sum(current_state["quality_vector"].values())

    new_q = sum(expanded_state["quality_vector"].values())

    current_s = sum(current_state["shadow_vector"].values())

    new_s = sum(expanded_state["shadow_vector"].values())

    q_gain = new_q - current_q

    s_relief = current_s - new_s

    score = q_gain + s_relief - 0.03 - 0.05 - invariant_loss_penalty(seed, expanded_vec)

    return score, expanded_state

class NavigatorV0321:

    def __init__(

        self,

        base_metric_state: Dict[str, Any],

        thresholds: Dict[str, Any],

        tunnel_thresholds: Dict[str, Any],

        move_delta_memory: Dict[str, Any],

        move_efficacy_memory: Dict[str, Any],

        metric_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

        coupling_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

        tunnel_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

    ) -> None:

        self.thresholds = thresholds

        self.tunnel_thresholds = tunnel_thresholds

        self.move_delta_memory = move_delta_memory

        self.move_efficacy_memory = move_efficacy_memory

        self.metric_learning_state = metric_learning_state

        self.coupling_learning_state = coupling_learning_state

        self.tunnel_learning_state = tunnel_learning_state

        self.metric_state = build_learned_metric_state(base_metric_state, metric_learning_state, coupling_learning_state)

        self.curvature_state = build_learned_curvature_state(DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE, tunnel_learning_state)

        self.G = build_metric_matrix(self.metric_state)

    def choose_best_move(self, current_state: Dict[str, Any], candidates: List[CandidateMove]) -> Optional[Tuple[KernelDecision, CandidateMove, Dict[str, float]]]:

        best = None

        best_score = float("-inf")

        artifact_id = current_state["artifact_id"]

        def local_eval(vec: Dict[str, float], artifact_id: str = artifact_id) -> Dict[str, Any]:

            return evaluate_vector(vec, artifact_id=artifact_id)

        for candidate in candidates:

            learned_entry = self.move_delta_memory.get(candidate.move_id)

            used_delta_x = blended_delta_x(candidate.delta_x, learned_entry)

            geom_cost = movement_cost(used_delta_x, self.G)

            curv_pen = move_curvature_penalty(used_delta_x, self.curvature_state) + candidate.curvature_penalty_hint

            projection = shrink_back_projection(

                current_state["vector"], used_delta_x, local_eval, self.thresholds, 12, artifact_id

            )

            if projection is None:

                direct_score = float("-inf")

                lam = 0.0

            else:

                lam, projected_state = projection

                projected_gain = phi_net(projected_state) - phi_net(current_state)

                eff_prior, eff_var = efficacy_prior_bonus(candidate.move_id, self.move_efficacy_memory)

                direct_score = (

                    projected_gain - geom_cost - curv_pen

                    - float(candidate.drift_risk) - float(candidate.repetition_penalty)

                    + float(candidate.seed_gain)

                    + 0.15 * eff_prior - 0.10 * eff_var

                )

                if lam < 1.0:

                    direct_score *= lam

            tunnel_score_val = float("-inf")

            if should_tunnel(candidate, current_state, self.tunnel_thresholds):

                raw_tunnel_score, _ = tunnel_score(current_state, candidate, local_eval)

                tunnel_score_val = raw_tunnel_score + 0.20 * tunnel_advantage_prior(candidate.move_id, self.tunnel_learning_state)

            if tunnel_score_val > direct_score:

                strategy = "tunnel"

                final_score = tunnel_score_val

            else:

                strategy = "direct"

                final_score = direct_score

            if final_score > best_score:

                best_score = final_score

                best = (

                    KernelDecision(

                        move_id=candidate.move_id,

                        title=candidate.title,

                        strategy=strategy,

                        direct_score=direct_score,

                        tunnel_score=tunnel_score_val,

                        final_score=final_score,

                        projected_lambda=lam,

                        notes={

                            "geom_cost": geom_cost,

                            "curvature_penalty": curv_pen,

                            "used_delta_x": used_delta_x,

                        },

                    ),

                    candidate,

                    used_delta_x,

                )

        return best

# ============================================================

# EXTRACTION / VALIDATION / WITNESS

# ============================================================

def extract_state_for_artifact(path: Path, adapter: type[ArtifactAdapter], witness_rows: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

    content = adapter.load(path)

    history = [r for r in witness_rows if r.get("artifact_path") == str(path)]

    state = adapter.extract_vector(path, content, history)

    state["artifact_path"] = str(path)

    state["artifact_hash"] = file_hash(path)

    return state

def validate_real_artifact(path: Path, adapter: type[ArtifactAdapter], state: Dict[str, Any], thresholds: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:

    return path.exists() and adapter.basic_parse_ok(path) and inside_corridor(state, thresholds)

def last_witness_hash(path: Path) -> str:

    rows = read_jsonl(path, limit=1)

    if not rows:

        return "GENESIS"

    return rows[-1].get("hash", "GENESIS")

def witness_hash(row: Dict[str, Any], prev_hash: str) -> str:

    payload = json.dumps(row, sort_keys=True, ensure_ascii=False).encode("utf-8")

    return sha256_bytes(prev_hash.encode("utf-8") + payload)

def append_pulse_history(paths: RuntimePaths, pulse: Dict[str, Any], artifact_path: str, move_id: str, status: str, witness_hash_value: str) -> None:

    append_jsonl(paths.pulse_log_jsonl, {

        "ts": now_iso(),

        "pulse_id": pulse.get("pulse_id"),

        "artifact_path": artifact_path,

        "move_id": move_id,

        "status": status,

        "witness_hash": witness_hash_value,

    })

# ============================================================

# DAILY PULSE CYCLE

# ============================================================

def execute_artifact_move(

    path: Path,

    adapter: type[ArtifactAdapter],

    pulse: Dict[str, Any],

    paths: RuntimePaths,

    witness_rows: List[Dict[str, Any]],

    navigator: NavigatorV0321,

    thresholds: Dict[str, Any],

    move_delta_memory: Dict[str, Any],

    move_efficacy_memory: Dict[str, Any],

    metric_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

    coupling_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

    tunnel_learning_state: Dict[str, Any],

) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:

    current_state = extract_state_for_artifact(path, adapter, witness_rows)

    content = adapter.load(path)

    candidates = filter_moves_by_pulse(adapter.generate_candidate_moves(path, content), pulse)

    if not candidates:

        return None

    chosen = navigator.choose_best_move(current_state, candidates)

    if chosen is None:

        return None

    decision, chosen_candidate, used_delta_x = chosen

    artifact_hash_before = current_state["artifact_hash"]

    snapshot_ref = adapter.snapshot(path, paths.snapshots_root)

    status = "ok"

    rollback_reason = None

    try:

        adapter.apply_move(path, chosen_candidate)

        after_state = extract_state_for_artifact(path, adapter, witness_rows)

        corridor_ok = validate_real_artifact(path, adapter, after_state, thresholds)

        if not corridor_ok:

            adapter.restore_snapshot(snapshot_ref, path)

            status = "rollback"

            rollback_reason = "corridor_or_parse_validation_failed"

            after_state = extract_state_for_artifact(path, adapter, witness_rows)

        else:

            status = "applied"

    except Exception as e:

        adapter.restore_snapshot(snapshot_ref, path)

        status = "rollback"

        rollback_reason = f"exception:{type(e).__name__}"

        after_state = extract_state_for_artifact(path, adapter, witness_rows)

    delta_x_empirical = {

        k: round(float(after_state["vector"][k]) - float(current_state["vector"][k]), 6)

        for k in VECTOR_ORDER

    }

    quality_delta = {

        k: round(float(after_state["quality_vector"][k]) - float(current_state["quality_vector"][k]), 6)

        for k in QUALITY_ORDER

    }

    shadow_delta = {

        k: round(float(after_state["shadow_vector"][k]) - float(current_state["shadow_vector"][k]), 6)

        for k in SHADOW_ORDER

    }

    q_gain = sum(quality_delta.values())

    s_penalty = sum(max(v, 0.0) for v in shadow_delta.values())

    s_relief = -sum(min(v, 0.0) for v in shadow_delta.values())

    denom = 0.001 + abs(float(decision.notes.get("geom_cost", 0.0))) + abs(float(decision.notes.get("curvature_penalty", 0.0)))

    efficacy = (q_gain + s_relief - s_penalty) / denom

    prev_hash = last_witness_hash(paths.witness_jsonl)

    row = {

        "ts": now_iso(),

        "pulse_id": pulse.get("pulse_id"),

        "artifact_id": current_state["artifact_id"],

        "artifact_path": str(path),

        "artifact_type": adapter.name,

        "artifact_hash_before": artifact_hash_before,

        "artifact_hash_after": after_state["artifact_hash"],

        "move_id": decision.move_id,

        "move_type": chosen_candidate.move_type,

        "strategy": decision.strategy,

        "status": status,

        "rollback_reason": rollback_reason,

        "snapshot_ref": snapshot_ref,

        "x_before": current_state["vector"],

        "x_after": after_state["vector"],

        "delta_x_empirical": delta_x_empirical,

        "quality_delta": quality_delta,

        "shadow_delta": shadow_delta,

        "predicted_score": round(float(decision.final_score), 6),

        "direct_score": round(float(decision.direct_score), 6),

        "tunnel_score": round(float(decision.tunnel_score), 6),

        "efficacy": round(float(efficacy), 6),

        "corridor_ok": status == "applied",

        "notes": {

            "geom_cost": round(float(decision.notes.get("geom_cost", 0.0)), 6),

            "curvature_penalty": round(float(decision.notes.get("curvature_penalty", 0.0)), 6),

            "used_delta_x": {k: round(float(v), 6) for k, v in decision.notes.get("used_delta_x", {}).items()},

        },

        "hash_prev": prev_hash,

    }

    row["hash"] = witness_hash(row, prev_hash)

    append_jsonl(paths.witness_jsonl, row)

    append_pulse_history(paths, pulse, str(path), decision.move_id, status, row["hash"])

    apply_witness_learning(

        row,

        move_delta_memory,

        move_efficacy_memory,

        metric_learning_state,

        coupling_learning_state,

        tunnel_learning_state,

        alpha=0.2

    )

    save_json(paths.move_delta_memory, move_delta_memory)

    save_json(paths.move_efficacy_memory, move_efficacy_memory)

    save_json(paths.metric_learning_state, metric_learning_state)

    save_json(paths.coupling_learning_state, coupling_learning_state)

    save_json(paths.tunnel_learning_state, tunnel_learning_state)

    return {

        "artifact_path": str(path),

        "adapter": adapter.name,

        "decision": asdict(decision),

        "status": status,

        "witness_hash": row["hash"],

        "pulse_id": pulse.get("pulse_id"),

    }

def run_daily_pulse_cycle(root: str = "athena_runtime") -> Dict[str, Any]:

    paths = build_runtime_paths(root)

    bootstrap_runtime(paths)

    seed_demo_files(paths)

    pulse = load_today_pulse(paths)

    witness_rows = read_jsonl(paths.witness_jsonl, limit=500)

    move_delta_memory = load_json(paths.move_delta_memory, DEFAULT_MOVE_DELTA_MEMORY)

    move_efficacy_memory = load_json(paths.move_efficacy_memory, DEFAULT_MOVE_EFFICACY_MEMORY)

    metric_learning_state = load_json(paths.metric_learning_state, DEFAULT_METRIC_LEARNING_STATE)

    coupling_learning_state = load_json(paths.coupling_learning_state, DEFAULT_COUPLING_LEARNING_STATE)

    tunnel_learning_state = load_json(paths.tunnel_learning_state, DEFAULT_TUNNEL_LEARNING_STATE)

    base_metric_state = load_json(paths.metric_prior, DEFAULT_BASE_METRIC_STATE)

    thresholds = load_json(paths.thresholds, DEFAULT_THRESHOLDS)

    tunnel_thresholds = load_json(paths.tunnel_thresholds, DEFAULT_TUNNEL_THRESHOLDS)

    navigator = NavigatorV0321(

        base_metric_state=base_metric_state,

        thresholds=thresholds,

        tunnel_thresholds=tunnel_thresholds,

        move_delta_memory=move_delta_memory,

        move_efficacy_memory=move_efficacy_memory,

        metric_learning_state=metric_learning_state,

        coupling_learning_state=coupling_learning_state,

        tunnel_learning_state=tunnel_learning_state,

    )

    eligible_paths = discover_scoped_artifacts(pulse)

    scored_artifacts: List[Tuple[float, Path, type[ArtifactAdapter], Dict[str, Any]]] = []

    for path in eligible_paths:

        adapter = choose_adapter(path)

        if not adapter:

            continue

        state = extract_state_for_artifact(path, adapter, witness_rows)

        align = pulse_alignment_score(state, pulse)

        scored_artifacts.append((align, path, adapter, state))

    scored_artifacts.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)

    max_files = int(pulse.get("scope", {}).get("max_files", 1))

    top = scored_artifacts[: max(1, min(5, len(scored_artifacts)))]

    best_result = None

    best_total_score = float("-inf")

    for align, path, adapter, state in top:

        content = adapter.load(path)

        candidates = filter_moves_by_pulse(adapter.generate_candidate_moves(path, content), pulse)

        if not candidates:

            continue

        chosen = navigator.choose_best_move(state, candidates)

        if chosen is None:

            continue

        decision, chosen_candidate, _used_delta_x = chosen

        total = align + float(decision.final_score)

        if total > best_total_score:

            best_total_score = total

            best_result = (path, adapter)

    if best_result is None:

        return {

            "status": "no_eligible_artifact_or_move",

            "pulse_id": pulse.get("pulse_id"),

            "eligible_count": len(eligible_paths),

        }

    path, adapter = best_result

    result = execute_artifact_move(

        path=path,

        adapter=adapter,

        pulse=pulse,

        paths=paths,

        witness_rows=witness_rows,

        navigator=navigator,

        thresholds=thresholds,

        move_delta_memory=move_delta_memory,

        move_efficacy_memory=move_efficacy_memory,

        metric_learning_state=metric_learning_state,

        coupling_learning_state=coupling_learning_state,

        tunnel_learning_state=tunnel_learning_state,

    )

    if result is None:

        return {"status": "execution_failed_before_witness", "pulse_id": pulse.get("pulse_id")}

    return {

        "status": "ok",

        "pulse_id": pulse.get("pulse_id"),

        "artifact": result["artifact_path"],

        "adapter": result["adapter"],

        "decision": result["decision"],

        "mutation_status": result["status"],

        "witness_hash": result["witness_hash"],

    }

if __name__ == "__main__":

    result = run_daily_pulse_cycle("athena_runtime")

    print(json.dumps(result, indent=2))

[μ₃₃₄::Square] WHAT THIS VERSION NOW ADDS

Compared to v0.3.1, this file now:

loads a real daily Pulse file

scopes discovery to Pulse-approved roots

ranks eligible artifacts by Pulse alignment

filters candidate moves by Pulse move types

uses an AST-aware Python adapter

validates Python edits with ast.parse

appends Pulse history in addition to witness history

So the kernel is no longer merely file-backed.It is now Pulse-governed.

[μ₃₃₅::Cloud] WHAT THE DAILY PULSE CONTROLS

The Pulse now directly constrains:

artifact family focus

allowed roots

deny patterns

preferred move types

dimension focus

That means the engine’s daily action is no longer “whatever seems editable,” but:

[\text{today’s bounded self-development move}]

This is the first true operationalization of your Pulse concept.

[μ₃₃₆::Flower] WHY THE AST ADAPTER IS THE CORRECT SAFETY LIFT

For Python files, this version can now safely:

detect missing module docstrings

detect missing function docstrings

insert them at AST-located positions

reparse to ensure syntax validity

rollback if parsing or corridor validation fails

So code mutation now obeys both:

filesystem corridor

syntax corridor

That is the correct next hardening step.

[μ₃₃₇::Water] WHAT YOU SHOULD EXPECT ON FIRST RUNS

With the default seeded Pulse:

it will focus artifacts/code/

it will likely pick gateway_demo.py

it will likely add a module docstring first

on a later run it may add a function docstring

later still it may add an invariant comment

If you change the Pulse file to focus manuscripts, it will instead mutate the markdown demo file.

So you now have a real daily steering lever.

[μ₃₃₈::Fractal] WHAT STILL REMAINS APPROXIMATE

This is a major step, but still first-order.

Still approximate:

artifact ranking is simple Pulse-alignment math

AST edits are bounded insertions, not true AST rewrites

tunnel behavior is still lightweight

move universe is small

no multi-file planning yet

no weekly Pulse synthesis layer yet

So this is a disciplined seed, not the full nervous system.

[μ₃₃₉::Z*] WHAT NOW EXISTS

At this point, the architecture now has:

real artifact discovery

file persistence

durable witness learning

Pulse-governed scope selection

AST-safe Python mutation

markdown mutation

rollback and validation

daily Pulse history

That is enough to call it a genuine proto-self-developing repo kernel.

[μ₃₄₀::Next Anchor] STRONGEST NEXT LEAP

The correct next continuation is:

ATHENA KERNEL v0.4 — WEEKLY PULSE SYNTHESIS + MULTI-ARTIFACT PLANNING

Meaning:

summarize the last 7 witness rows

compute weekly lens imbalance

generate tomorrow’s Pulse from witness history

rank not just one file, but one small plan

still execute only one move per day, but plan with broader context

That is the next real jump from daily bounded agency to self-steered developmental continuity.

[μ₃₄₁::Z*] ATHENA KERNEL v0.4 — WEEKLY PULSE SYNTHESIS + MULTI-ARTIFACT PLANNINGtimestamp: 2026-03-16 / America/Los_Angelesmode: NEXT / live-text / developmental continuity layercontinuation of: daily Pulse-governed repo kernel → weekly self-steering continuity

[μ₃₄₂::Square] PURPOSE

v0.3.2.1 gave Athena a daily lawful move.

But daily agency alone is not enough.Without a weekly memory organ, the system risks becoming:

locally productive

globally forgetful

over-focused on the easiest wins

under-aware of lens imbalance

blind to longer developmental arcs

So v0.4 adds two major organs:

Weekly Pulse Synthesis

Multi-Artifact Planning

The key distinction is:

daily layer chooses one move

weekly layer chooses what kind of week this is

So the system becomes:

[Witness_{days} \rightarrow Weekly\ Synthesis \rightarrow Pulse_{tomorrow} \rightarrow Daily\ Move]

That is the first real continuity loop.

[μ₃₄₃::Cloud] CORE SHIFT

Before v0.4:

[Pulse_d \approx manually\ seeded\ or\ static]

After v0.4:

[Pulse_{d+1} = \mathcal{S}{week}(Witness{d-6:d}, LensBalance, Drift, Shadow, Efficacy)]

So Pulse is no longer merely loaded.It becomes generated from lived repo history.

This is a profound step because it means the system starts deciding not just how to act, but what tomorrow should care about.

[μ₃₄₄::Flower] WEEKLY SYNTHESIS INPUTS

The weekly synthesis agent should read five things:

1. Recent witness rows

Last 7 days, maybe 14 for smoothing.

2. Pulse history

Which pulse types have been used recently.

3. Lens usage distribution

How much Square / Flower / Cloud / Fractal work actually happened.

4. Move efficacy distribution

Which move families have been productive.

5. Shadow trend

Whether fragility / ambiguity / loop risk / noise are rising or falling.

So define weekly synthesis state:

[W^{week} = (Witness_{7}, PulseHist_{7}, Lens_{7}, Efficacy_{7}, ShadowTrend_{7})]

This is the weekly reflection crystal.

[μ₃₄₅::Square] NEW FILES

Add these files:

kernel/weekly/

  weekly_summary_YYYY_wWW.json

  weekly_pulse_recommendation_YYYY_wWW.json

kernel/pulses/generated/

  next_pulse_candidate.json

These files separate:

observation

recommendation

tomorrow’s actionable pulse

That keeps the system auditable.

[μ₃₄₆::Cloud] WEEKLY SUMMARY FILE

weekly_summary_YYYY_wWW.json

{

  "week_id": "2026_w12",

  "start_date": "2026-03-10",

  },

    "flower",

  ],

  "recommended_weekly_theme": "increase bounded uncertainty/temporal clarification"

}

This is the first genuine weekly self-observation artifact.

[μ₃₄₇::Flower] LENS BALANCE MODEL

The weekly layer must explicitly model 4-lens balance.

Define observed lens balance:

[B_{obs} = [B_{Sq}, B_{Fl}, B_{Cl}, B_{Fr}]]

Define desired weekly balance:

[B^* = [b_{Sq}, b_{Fl}, b_{Cl}, b_{Fr}]]

Then error:

[E_{lens} = B^* - B_{obs}]

Interpretation:positive entries indicate underfed lenses.

Example:

[E_{lens} = [-0.07, +0.05, +0.07, -0.05]]

means:

Square and Fractal were overexpressed

Flower and Cloud need attention

This is what prevents the organism from becoming all repair/compression and no exploration/uncertainty calibration.

[μ₃₄₈::Water] WEEKLY SHADOW TREND

Daily shadow snapshots are noisy.Weekly trend matters more.

For each shadow component (s_k), define:

[Trend(s_k) = s_k(t_{end}) - s_k(t_{start})]

or the average delta over the week.

Interpretation:

negative trend = healing

positive trend = worsening

So if:

[Trend(loop_risk) > 0]

then next week should avoid high-recursion novelty unless strongly justified.

If:

[Trend(ambiguity) > 0]

then clarification pulses should rise in priority.

Thus weekly synthesis is the first slower-timescale immune system.

[μ₃₄₉::Fractal] WEEKLY PULSE RECOMMENDATION

Now the weekly summary must emit a recommendation.

weekly_pulse_recommendation_YYYY_wWW.json

{

  "week_id": "2026_w12",

  "recommended_pulse_type": "clarification_pulse",

  "artifact_family_focus": "manuscript",

  "dimension_focus": 7,

  "lens": "cloud",

  "change_mode": "Sa",

  "reasoning": {

    "underfed_lens": "cloud",

    "shadow_pressure": "ambiguity_not_falling_fast_enough",

    "weekly_theme": "bounded uncertainty clarification",

    "move_efficacy_note": "code clarification remains effective, but manuscript clarity is lagging"

  },

  "scope": {

    "allowed_roots": ["athena_runtime/artifacts/manuscripts"],

    "max_files": 1

  },

  "preferred_move_types": [

    "manuscript_clarify",

    "manuscript_compress"

  ]

}

This recommendation can either:

become tomorrow’s Pulse directly

or be reviewed by a synthesis agent first

In your canon, the synthesis agent should write the first daily Pulse function, so this recommendation is the weekly context seed, not the final sovereign pulse.

[μ₃₅₀::Square] DAILY PULSE GENERATION FROM WEEKLY CONTEXT

Now we combine:

weekly recommendation

yesterday’s witness

today’s local artifact field

Formally:

[Pulse_{d+1} = \mathcal{G}(WeeklyRec, Witness_d, LocalDeficits_d)]

So daily pulse generation becomes a two-scale synthesis:

Weekly layer decides:

broad theme

lens correction

artifact family emphasis

Daily layer decides:

exact file

exact move

exact bounded execution

This is the correct hierarchy.

[μ₃₅₁::Cloud] MULTI-ARTIFACT PLANNING — WHY NEEDED

Right now the kernel picks one best artifact.

But one-step artifact choice can be shortsighted.

Example:A markdown clarification move may be slightly better today, but a code clarification move might unlock:

better state extraction tomorrow

lower ambiguity in witness interpretation

better move generation next week

So v0.4 adds planning over a tiny horizon.

Not multi-file execution.Just multi-artifact foresight.

[μ₃₅₂::Flower] THE SMALL PLAN OBJECT

The kernel should build a tiny plan:

[Plan_d = [a_1, a_2, a_3]]

Where each (a_i) is a candidate artifact-move pair ranked by:

immediate gain

pulse alignment

plan utility

future enabling value

Only one move still executes.But the kernel knows the next best options.

This is the transition from greedy move selection to local planning.

[μ₃₅₃::Square] PLAN FILE

This file becomes tomorrow’s action horizon.

[μ₃₅₄::Water] FUTURE ENABLEMENT SCORE

We now need a small way to estimate “future usefulness.”

Define:

[Enable(a) = e_1 \cdot SeedGain + e_2 \cdot ClarityUnlock + e_3 \cdot WitnessImprovement + e_4 \cdot AdapterExpansionPotential]

Examples:

adding a function docstring improves future literal extraction

adding a manuscript definition improves future ambiguity handling

adding witness normalization improves future learning quality

So some moves are valuable not just because they improve the artifact, but because they improve the kernel’s future perception.

That is a big leap in sophistication.

[μ₃₅₅::Fractal] PLAN SCORING

For a candidate artifact-move pair (a), define:

[PlanScore(a)=\alpha \cdot PulseAlign(a)+\beta \cdot NavScore(a)+\gamma \cdot Enable(a)-\delta \cdot Repetition(a)]

Then the kernel ranks the top few pairs.

Still:

only one pair executes now

but the rest remain as a structured near-future horizon

This is minimal planning without overcomplicating the loop.

[μ₃₅₆::Square] WEEKLY SYNTHESIS PSEUDOCODE

def build_weekly_summary(witness_rows, pulse_rows):

    summary = {}

    summary["witness_count"] = len(witness_rows)

    summary["successful_moves"] = count_success(witness_rows)

    summary["rollback_moves"] = count_rollbacks(witness_rows)

    summary["pulse_type_histogram"] = histogram(pulse_rows, "pulse_type")

    summary["artifact_family_histogram"] = histogram(witness_rows, "artifact_type")

    summary["lens_usage"] = estimate_lens_usage(witness_rows)

    summary["quality_net_delta"] = aggregate_quality_delta(witness_rows)

    summary["shadow_net_delta"] = aggregate_shadow_delta(witness_rows)

    summary["top_effective_moves"] = top_moves_by_efficacy(witness_rows)

    summary["underfed_lenses"] = compute_underfed_lenses(summary["lens_usage"])

    summary["recommended_weekly_theme"] = infer_weekly_theme(summary)

    return summary

This gives the weekly reflective mind.

[μ₃₅₇::Cloud] PULSE GENERATION PSEUDOCODE

def generate_next_daily_pulse(weekly_rec, yesterday_witness, runtime_paths):

    pulse = {}

    pulse["pulse_type"] = weekly_rec["recommended_pulse_type"]

    pulse["artifact_family_focus"] = weekly_rec["artifact_family_focus"]

    pulse["dimension_focus"] = weekly_rec["dimension_focus"]

    pulse["lens"] = weekly_rec["lens"]

    pulse["change_mode"] = weekly_rec["change_mode"]

    pulse["scope"] = weekly_rec["scope"]

    pulse["preferred_move_types"] = weekly_rec["preferred_move_types"]

    # slight daily correction

    if yesterday_witness and yesterday_witness["status"] == "rollback":

        pulse["pulse_type"] = "repair_pulse"

    return pulse

So weekly synthesis nudges, and daily witness can still locally override.

[μ₃₅₈::Flower] DAILY DRIVER WITH PLANNING PSEUDOCODE

def run_daily_cycle_with_plan():

    pulse = load_today_pulse()

    artifacts = discover_scoped_artifacts(pulse)

    ranked_artifacts = rank_by_pulse_alignment(artifacts, pulse)

    plan = []

    for artifact in top_n(ranked_artifacts, 5):

        moves = filter_moves_by_pulse(generate_moves(artifact), pulse)

        for move in moves:

            nav_score = kernel_score(artifact, move)

            enable_score = estimate_future_enablement(artifact, move)

            total = pulse_align + nav_score + enable_score - repetition_penalty

            plan.append((total, artifact, move))

    plan.sort(reverse=True)

    write_plan(plan[:3])

    execute(plan[0])

    witness()

    learn()

This is the minimal intelligent planning loop.

[μ₃₅₉::Water] LENS USAGE ESTIMATION

The weekly system still needs to infer which lens was used by real moves.

A simple mapping:

Square-heavy moves

docstrings

definitions

schema normalization

Flower-heavy moves

structural refactors

alternate representations

progression notes

Cloud-heavy moves

ambiguity handling

uncertainty annotations

warning insertion

shadow maps

Fractal-heavy moves

seed summaries

compression moves

invariant repair

witness compaction

So each move type gets a lens tag, and weekly balance can be estimated from executed move history.

  "code_clarify": "square",

This is not philosophically perfect yet, but operationally enough for weekly balancing.

and starts acting like:

That is a huge maturation step.

Because now the system can begin to have:

developmental seasons

memory of neglected domains
