[μ₃₆₇::Fractal] athena_kernel_v041.py

from __future__ import annotations

import ast

import os

import json

import math

import copy

import hashlib

from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict, field

from datetime import datetime, timedelta

from pathlib import Path

from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional, Tuple

# ============================================================

# CANONICAL ORDERS

# ============================================================

VECTOR_ORDER = ["L", "S", "T", "C", "A", "N", "U", "R", "M", "P", "H", "Z"]

QUALITY_ORDER = [

    "truth", "coherence", "novelty", "utility",

    "compression", "safety", "vitality", "recoverability"

]

SHADOW_ORDER = [

    "hallucination", "fragility", "drift", "ambiguity",

    "coupling", "vanity", "noise", "loop_risk"

]

MOVE_LENS_MAP = {

    "code_clarify": "square",

    "code_repair": "fractal",

    "manuscript_clarify": "square",

    "manuscript_compress": "fractal",

    "witness_normalize": "cloud",

    "state_regenerate": "flower",

}

DESIRED_WEEKLY_LENS_BALANCE = {

    "square": 0.25,

    "flower": 0.25,

    "cloud": 0.25,

    "fractal": 0.25,

}

# ============================================================

# BASIC UTILS

# ============================================================

def clamp01(x: float) -> float:

    return max(0.0, min(1.0, float(x)))

def squash(x: float) -> float:

    return 1.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-x))

def mean(xs: List[float], default: float = 0.0) -> float:

    return sum(xs) / len(xs) if xs else default

def variance(xs: List[float], default: float = 0.0) -> float:

    if not xs:

        return default

    m = mean(xs)

    return sum((x - m) ** 2 for x in xs) / len(xs)

def now_iso() -> str:

    return datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z"

def iso_date() -> str:

    return datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y-%m-%d")

def ensure_dir(path: str | Path) -> None:

    Path(path).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def load_json(path: str | Path, default: Any) -> Any:

    p = Path(path)

    if not p.exists():

        return copy.deepcopy(default)

    try:

        with p.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:

            return json.load(f)

    except Exception:

        return copy.deepcopy(default)

def save_json(path: str | Path, obj: Any) -> None:

    p = Path(path)

    ensure_dir(p.parent)

    tmp = p.with_suffix(p.suffix + ".tmp")

    with tmp.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:

        json.dump(obj, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

    tmp.replace(p)

def append_jsonl(path: str | Path, row: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:

    p = Path(path)

    ensure_dir(p.parent)

    with p.open("a", encoding="utf-8") as f:

        f.write(json.dumps(row, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")

def read_jsonl(path: str | Path, limit: int = 500) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:

    p = Path(path)

    if not p.exists():

        return []

    rows: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []

    with p.open("r", encoding="utf-8") as f:

        for line in f:

            line = line.strip()

            if not line:

                continue

            try:

                rows.append(json.loads(line))

            except Exception:

                continue

    return rows[-limit:]

def sha256_bytes(b: bytes) -> str:

    return "sha256:" + hashlib.sha256(b).hexdigest()

def file_hash(path: str | Path) -> str:

    with open(path, "rb") as f:

        return sha256_bytes(f.read())

def add_delta(x: Dict[str, float], delta_x: Dict[str, float], lam: float = 1.0) -> Dict[str, float]:

    out = dict(x)

    for k, v in delta_x.items():

        out[k] = clamp01(float(out.get(k, 0.0)) + lam * float(v))

    return out

def vector_dict_to_list(d: Dict[str, float], order: List[str]) -> List[float]:

    return [float(d.get(k, 0.0)) for k in order]

def shadow_total(shadow_vector: Dict[str, float]) -> float:

    return sum(float(shadow_vector.get(k, 0.0)) for k in SHADOW_ORDER) / max(1, len(SHADOW_ORDER))

def week_id_now() -> str:

    year, week, _ = datetime.utcnow().isocalendar()

    return f"{year}_w{week:02d}"

# ============================================================

# QUALITY / SHADOW

# ============================================================

QUALITY_WEIGHTS = {

    "truth": 1.00,

    "coherence": 0.95,

    "novelty": 0.72,

    "utility": 0.90,

    "compression": 0.78,

    "safety": 1.05,

    "vitality": 0.80,

    "recoverability": 1.00,

}

SHADOW_WEIGHTS = {

    "hallucination": 1.10,

    "fragility": 1.00,

    "drift": 0.90,

    "ambiguity": 0.95,

    "coupling": 0.82,

    "vanity": 0.76,

    "noise": 0.74,

    "loop_risk": 1.02,

}

def derive_quality_vector(vector: Dict[str, float]) -> Dict[str, float]:

    novelty_raw = 0.30 * (1.0 - vector["T"]) + 0.35 * vector["A"] + 0.35 * vector["P"]

    return {

        "truth": clamp01(0.35 * vector["L"] + 0.20 * vector["U"] + 0.20 * vector["N"] + 0.25 * vector["C"]),

        "coherence": clamp01(0.45 * vector["S"] + 0.20 * vector["C"] + 0.15 * vector["A"] + 0.20 * vector["Z"]),

        "novelty": clamp01(novelty_raw),

        "utility": clamp01(0.35 * vector["L"] + 0.25 * vector["C"] + 0.20 * vector["H"] + 0.20 * vector["M"]),

        "compression": clamp01(0.65 * vector["P"] + 0.35 * vector["Z"]),

        "safety": clamp01(0.20 * vector["N"] + 0.25 * vector["U"] + 0.25 * vector["H"] + 0.30 * vector["R"]),

        "vitality": clamp01(0.30 * vector["T"] + 0.20 * vector["A"] + 0.20 * vector["M"] + 0.30 * vector["Z"]),

        "recoverability": clamp01(0.65 * vector["H"] + 0.35 * vector["Z"]),

    }

def derive_shadow_vector(vector: Dict[str, float]) -> Dict[str, float]:

    return {

        "hallucination": clamp01(1.0 - 0.6 * vector["L"] - 0.4 * vector["U"]),

        "fragility": clamp01(1.0 - 0.7 * vector["H"] - 0.3 * vector["R"]),

        "drift": clamp01(1.0 - vector["T"]),

        "ambiguity": clamp01(1.0 - 0.5 * vector["L"] - 0.5 * vector["A"]),

        "coupling": clamp01(1.0 - 0.6 * vector["C"] - 0.4 * vector["S"]),

        "vanity": clamp01(1.0 - 0.5 * vector["N"] - 0.5 * vector["U"]),

        "noise": clamp01(1.0 - 0.5 * vector["P"] - 0.5 * vector["Z"]),

        "loop_risk": clamp01(1.0 - vector["R"]),

    }

def phi_quality(q: Dict[str, float]) -> float:

    return sum(float(q[k]) * QUALITY_WEIGHTS[k] for k in QUALITY_ORDER)

def phi_shadow(s: Dict[str, float]) -> float:

    return sum(float(s[k]) * SHADOW_WEIGHTS[k] for k in SHADOW_ORDER)

def phi_net(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> float:

    return phi_quality(state["quality_vector"]) - phi_shadow(state["shadow_vector"])

def evaluate_vector(vector: Dict[str, float], artifact_id: str = "artifact") -> Dict[str, Any]:

    vec = {k: clamp01(float(vector.get(k, 0.0))) for k in VECTOR_ORDER}

    q = derive_quality_vector(vec)

    s = derive_shadow_vector(vec)

    return {

        "artifact_id": artifact_id,

        "vector": vec,

        "quality_vector": q,

        "shadow_vector": s,

        "invariants": {"role": "generic", "reversible": True},

    }

# ============================================================

# METRIC / CURVATURE

# ============================================================

def zeros(n: int) -> List[List[float]]:

    return [[0.0 for _ in range(n)] for _ in range(n)]

def symmetrize(M: List[List[float]]) -> List[List[float]]:

    n = len(M)

    out = zeros(n)

    for i in range(n):

        for j in range(n):

            out[i][j] = 0.5 * (M[i][j] + M[j][i])

    return out

def clamp_min_diag(M: List[List[float]], floor: float = 1e-3) -> List[List[float]]:

    out = [row[:] for row in M]

    for i in range(len(M)):

        if out[i][i] < floor:

            out[i][i] = floor

    return out

def build_metric_matrix(metric_state: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[List[float]]:

    idx = {k: i for i, k in enumerate(VECTOR_ORDER)}

    G = zeros(len(VECTOR_ORDER))

    for dim, val in metric_state.get("diagonal", {}).items():

        G[idx[dim]][idx[dim]] = float(val)

    for pair, val in metric_state.get("couplings", {}).items():

        left, right = pair.split(":")

        i, j = idx[left], idx[right]

        G[i][j] = float(val)

        G[j][i] = float(val)

    return clamp_min_diag(symmetrize(G))

def quad_form(v: List[float], G: List[List[float]]) -> float:

    total = 0.0

    n = len(v)

    for i in range(n):

        for j in range(n):

            total += v[i] * G[i][j] * v[j]

    return total

def movement_cost(delta_x: Dict[str, float], G: List[List[float]]) -> float:

    v = vector_dict_to_list(delta_x, VECTOR_ORDER)

    return math.sqrt(max(0.0, quad_form(v, G)))

def move_curvature_penalty(delta_x: Dict[str, float], K: Dict[str, Dict[str, float]]) -> float:

    dims = [k for k, v in delta_x.items() if abs(v) > 1e-12]

    total = 0.0

    for i in dims:

        for j in dims:

            if i == j:

                continue

            total += abs(float(delta_x[i]) * float(delta_x[j])) * float(K.get(i, {}).get(j, 0.0))

    return total

DEFAULT_BASE_METRIC_STATE = {

    "diagonal": {

        "L": 1.00, "S": 1.10, "T": 1.05, "C": 1.15,

        "A": 0.95, "N": 1.00, "U": 0.95, "R": 1.20,

        "M": 1.00, "P": 1.05, "H": 1.10, "Z": 1.15,

    },

    "couplings": {

        "L:S": 0.18, "S:C": 0.21, "C:H": 0.24, "N:U": 0.19,

        "R:M": 0.22, "P:Z": 0.26, "H:Z": 0.17, "T:R": 0.16, "A:M": 0.12,

    },

}

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE = {d: {e: 0.0 for e in VECTOR_ORDER} for d in VECTOR_ORDER}

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["R"]["M"] = DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["M"]["R"] = 0.40

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["C"]["H"] = DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["H"]["C"] = 0.31

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["P"]["Z"] = DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["Z"]["P"] = 0.28

DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["T"]["R"] = DEFAULT_BASE_CURVATURE["R"]["T"] = 0.25

# ============================================================

# RUNTIME PATHS
